# FIELD_NOTES.md
Last updated: 2026-07-23 (google-sheet-products-for-shop v0.1.20: Pull/Push errors now say what actually failed (Google API detail or the real thrown reason) instead of one generic "could not read the sheet" line; new SheetsApiError/sheetFailureReason in lib/sheets.ts. **Suppliers now carry their own catalogues.** New `shp_supplier_catalogues` table (shop `010_supplier_catalogues.sql`, v0.1.91) - name + optional Google Sheet URL + position, FK to `shp_suppliers` ON DELETE CASCADE, unique on `(supplier_id, LOWER(name))`; edited as a repeating block in the Suppliers form and written whole with `replaceSupplierCatalogues` (delete-then-insert in one transaction). google-sheet-products-for-shop v0.1.19 adds a fourth workbook tab, **Supplier Catalogues**, written on every Push and never read by Pull; workbooks made before it existed grow it on their next Push via the new `addTab`/`ensureSupplierCataloguesTab`. Backup gate re-run for the new table: schema-coverage green, round-trip **real PASS (3/3)**. **Staff email change is now two-step.** `POST /api/account/email` no longer writes the new address: it parks it on an `EmailChallenge` (new nullable `pendingEmail` column - init migration edited in place plus idempotent `prisma/core-reconcile/011_email_change_pending.sql`, new `email_change` purpose and `email_change` rate-limit action) and posts a code to the new address; `PUT` confirms it and only then moves `User.email`, stamping `emailVerifiedAt` because the code proves control. The old address is notified (`sendEmailChangeNotice`), best-effort so an unreachable old mailbox cannot block the change. Members are unaffected - they have no self-service email change. **Pre-order stock moved to the dispatch path.** `createShipment` now decrements stock for pre-order lines by the units in THAT parcel, inside its existing transaction and advisory lock; the SHIPPED transition records an implicit shipment for whatever is still outstanding instead of decrementing itself, and `deleteShipment` gives the stock back. Exactly one decrement per unit - normal lines are still counted at payment only. **Stranded refunds are reconciled, not guessed.** `reconcileStaleRefunds` in `modules/shop/lib/db/refunds.ts` plus daily cron `modules/shop/app/api/cron/reconcile-refunds/route.ts`; new optional `getRefundStatus` on `ShpPaymentProvider` (implemented for Stripe, which now stamps `metadata.shpRefundId` on the refund; GoCardless and PayPal have no implementation yet and their rows are reported to the owner rather than settled). The intended breakdown is persisted at PENDING time in a new `shp_refunds.intended_items` JSONB column (migration `009_refund_intended_items.sql`, folded into 001) because `shp_refund_items` is deliberately written only on success. **Backup aborts on a FK cycle.** `topoSortTables` used to append tables it could not order, emitting a file that only failed at restore; it now throws the new `UnrestorableBackupError` (`lib/backup/serialize.ts`, surfaced by the backup route), covered by `lib/backup/dump.topo.test.ts`. Self-referencing FKs were already handled at row level and were not a bug. **Deploy status is keyed on the right deployment.** `getLatestDeploymentStatus(deploymentId?)` prefers `SiteConfig.pendingRedeployId` over "the project's newest deployment", so an unrelated push can no longer be mistaken for this install's outcome. **Failed/inactive modules no longer ship.** `lib/deploy/redeploy.ts` excludes those two statuses from `modules.json`, which previously shipped code for modules `run-module-migrations.mjs` never migrates - live routes over missing tables. **Generators trust the registry.** New `scripts/lib/module-names.mjs`, used by all seven `generate-module-*.mjs`, filters module directories against `modules.json` rather than listing the folder (a stale checkout used to be wired into local builds); nothing is ever deleted. `contact-form-reply-catcher` was on disk but unregistered, so it is now pinned in `modules.json` at v0.1.7 (repo `cactus-foundation-modules/reply-catcher`). **PayPal part-refunds.** `PAYMENT.CAPTURE.REFUNDED` fires for partial refunds too, so the handler now compares the cumulative refunded amount against the order total and reports `PARTIALLY_REFUNDED` rather than always `REFUNDED`. **Boards reserved slugs completed.** `RESERVED_BOARD_SLUGS` gained `tag` and `feed.xml` and is now used by the three routes that previously hardcoded `['t','u']`. **product-attributes has a settings tab at last** - new `components/SettingsTab.tsx` + `app/api/admin/settings/route.ts`, registered via manifest `settingsTabs`, exposing `hideEmptyValues` and `includeVariantValues`, neither of which had any UI. | **Shop: part-dispatch.** An order can now leave in more than one parcel. New `shp_shipments` / `shp_shipment_items` tables (migration `008_shipments.sql`, also folded into `001_initial.sql` for fresh installs), `modules/shop/lib/db/shipments.ts` (`createShipment`, `getShipmentsForOrder`, `getDispatchedQtyByOrderItem`, `getOrderDispatchSummary`, `isOrderFullyDispatched`, `deleteShipment`) and admin route `app/api/admin/orders/[id]/dispatch/route.ts` (POST records a dispatch, GET returns the dispatch summary + shipments + pre-order hold state, DELETE undoes a shipment). Dispatched quantity is DERIVED by summing shipment lines - there is deliberately no denormalised counter column - and the writes take the SAME advisory-lock namespace as refunds, because refunds and dispatch police the same units of the same order. `OrderDetailScreen.tsx` gains a Dispatched column, a "Dispatch items" action, a Dispatches list, a HOLD_ALL banner and a derived "Partly dispatched"/"All dispatched" marker (NOT a new order status value); new `components/admin/DispatchModal.tsx`. New `PARTIAL_SHIPPED` email trigger ("Part of an order dispatched") seeded in both 001 and 008 and sent via `lib/shipment-email.ts` (`sendShipmentDispatchedEmail`); its copy switches wording for the final parcel, so one template covers both cases and `STATUS_SHIPPED` is left for an owner flipping the whole order. `preOrderMixedCartBehaviour` is finally implemented, as a FULFILMENT policy rather than a checkout restriction: HOLD_ALL refuses to let the admin mark an order SHIPPED while pre-order lines are outstanding (409 with a plain-English explanation) and tells the shopper at checkout that the whole order ships together, PROMPT_SPLIT permits part-dispatch and says in-stock items can be sent straight away. A mixed basket stays purchasable either way. The shared rule `outstandingPreOrderItems` lives in `modules/shop/lib/db/orders.ts` so the status route (which enforces the hold) and the dispatch route (which explains it) cannot drift apart.) (**Shop: stock, coupon, refund and pre-order correctness.** Stock no longer under-decrements when a basket holds two lines of the same product - `decrementStockOnShip` aggregates `SUM … GROUP BY product_id` before joining, where the plain join updated each product row once regardless of how many lines pointed at it. Coupon usage is keyed on the resolved `coupon_id` rather than the raw code (`fulfillPaidOrder`, `countPriorCouponOrdersByEmail`, and the payment-intent route only stores `couponCode` when a coupon genuinely resolved), so a rejected or expired code no longer burns `usage_count` or a customer's per-customer allowance. Refunds go through new `processRefund` (`modules/shop/lib/db/refunds.ts`): validation happens under a transaction-scoped advisory lock with a committed PENDING reservation row, the provider HTTP call runs OUTSIDE any database transaction, the refund row id is passed to Stripe, PayPal and GoCardless as a deterministic idempotency key, and a FAILED provider refund no longer bumps `refunded_qty`. `markOrderPaymentFailed(id, reason)` now takes `'FAILED' | 'CHARGEBACK'`; a chargeback on an already-PAID order moves it to ON_HOLD with `payment_status='FAILED'` and an internal note instead of being silently ignored. Stripe's `charge.refunded` resolves the order via `charge.payment_intent` and the new `getOrderByPaymentReference` - the `shpOrderId` metadata it used to read only ever exists on the PaymentIntent, never on the Charge. Minimum/maximum order value is enforced at the order-creating payment-intent route, not just the checkout-session route. `updateOrderStatus` is idempotent and returns whether anything changed, so SHIPPED → COMPLETED → SHIPPED can no longer double-decrement pre-order stock. `pre_order_count` is released on a genuine cancellation via new `decrementPreOrderCount` (the refund settle path runs the same statement inlined, on its own transaction client), and both also re-enable a product the cap had auto-switched out of pre-order mode; previously the counter only ever went up, permanently consuming the allocation.) (**Core: scheme allow-list, media picker `?id=`, pre-auth payload.** New `isHttpUrl(value)` in `lib/utils.ts` - an http(s)-only scheme allow-list - closes a stored-XSS hole: a `javascript:` member `websiteUrl` was accepted by both write paths (`app/api/members/profile/route.ts`, `app/api/admin/members/[id]/route.ts`; Zod's `.url()` happily passes it) and rendered straight into an `href` on `app/(public)/members/[username]/page.tsx`. The same guard now gates the Puck Video and Embed blocks' iframe `src` in `lib/puck/config.tsx`. `GET /api/admin/media` honours an `?id=` parameter, returning that one row in the usual `{ items: [...] }` envelope - it previously ignored the parameter and fell through to the newest-first listing, so the media picker previewed the last-uploaded image instead of the chosen one. `GET /api/auth/config` no longer returns `neonProjectId` (infrastructure metadata has no business in a pre-auth payload) and `LoginForm.tsx` links to the plain Neon console instead. `proxy.ts`'s protected-role bypass wraps its response in `withSecurity()`, so a signed-in admin no longer browses a gated site with every security header missing.) (**Backups are now taken from one snapshot.** The entire read phase of `buildBackupSql` (`lib/backup/dump.ts`) runs inside a SINGLE `RepeatableRead`, `READ ONLY` interactive transaction (10s maxWait, 58s timeout - just under the route's 60s ceiling), so table discovery, every table's rows and the sequence counters all agree on one instant. A dump taken while the site was serving traffic could previously be torn - a sequence read at N while a row using N+1 was read afterwards, or a child row written mid-dump referencing a parent whose table had already been read - and that only ever surfaces at RESTORE. `BackupDb` therefore now requires `$transaction`, with a narrower `BackupTx` for the read helpers (an interactive transaction client has no `$transaction` of its own). `lib/backup/serialize.ts` gained real `date`/`time`/`timetz` handling: they were claimed as supported but sat in the string-only TEXTUAL set, and Prisma returns those columns as a JS `Date`, so the first install carrying a DATE column would have thrown `UnsupportedColumnError` and aborted its own backup.) (**Build scripts: no silent fallbacks.** `scripts/checkout-modules.mjs` no longer falls back to an unpinned HEAD clone for a PINNED module on Vercel - it retries the pinned clone once and then fails the build, rather than shipping unvetted module code (possibly needing a newer core) while the database and `modules.json` still claim the pin; local dev stays lenient so a deleted tag doesn't block work. The four `scripts/generate-module-*.mjs` generators (puck, settings-tabs, sms-providers, extension-points) dedupe emitted imports - a module contributing one component to two points emitted the same identifier twice, which does not compile - and throw when one identifier maps to two different import paths, which is a genuine name clash. `scripts/prebuild.mjs` exits non-zero when the checkout child is killed by a signal, instead of reading a null exit code as success.) (**Module repos: public endpoints and notification email.** contact-form HTML-escapes every submission field in the owner notification (escape first, then convert newlines to `<br>` - the other order lets a dangling `<` swallow the break tag) and its address check now rejects quotes and angle brackets. contact-form-reply-catcher no longer re-processes the newest mailbox message on every poll: the IMAP `maxUid+1:*` range always re-includes the highest UID, so `getProcessedUids` filters the already-recorded ones and replies stop duplicating. boards' reply endpoint honours thread moderation status, and poll votes, post reactions and reports now check board visibility and validate that the reported item exists and is visible to the reporter. gazette's reactions and views require a publicly visible post (`isPostPubliclyVisible`) and 404 cleanly instead of inflating counts on a draft or unknown id. product-3d-views-for-shop registers the `core.media-reference-rewriters` extension point and adds heal-on-read (`lib/media-reference-rewriter.ts`, `lib/db/heal.ts`), so a 3D model no longer 404s permanently after a product or folder rename. product-attributes-for-shop's filter counts respect the include-variant-values setting. google-sheet-products-for-shop serialises concurrent pull steps behind a transaction-scoped advisory lock and rejects negative prices on import, as does shop's own CSV import engine.) (**Module-system/deploy hardening.** DeployLock stale-lock auto-recovery via `getActiveDeployLock()` (`lib/deploy/lock.ts`, 15-min `STALE_LOCK_MS`) at every acquire/check site (install/update/core-update/uninstall) so a hard-killed function no longer strands a permanent 409; bulk "Update all" now runs the single-module compat gate per module via `checkModuleUpdateCompat()` (`lib/modules/compat.ts`) and drops incompatible modules into `failed[]` instead of pinning a build-breaking tag into `modules.json`; `fetchManifestFromRepo` reads the manifest at the `release.tag` being installed rather than HEAD; core-update blob fetches in `syncCoreFromUpstream` are now a bounded (8-wide) worker pool with a tighter per-blob retry budget so a large update fits the 60s ceiling instead of being hard-killed mid-push; factory hard-reset TRUNCATE now clears `GithubAppConnection`/`SavedBlock`/`Folder`/`Tag`/`Notification`/`EmailTemplate`.) (**Product: Tabs strip - background opacity now works without a picked colour, and its number boxes clear properly.** In `modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`, `navBgVars` previously returned nothing when `bgColour` was blank, so the "Background opacity (%)" field silently did nothing unless a colour was also chosen; with no colour it now thins the strip's default page-background fill (`color-mix` on `--color-page-bg`), so a sticky strip can go translucent on its own. `bgOpacity`/`padTop`/`padBottom` swapped from Puck's built-in number field (which stores `Number('') = 0` on a cleared box, trapping the value at 0) to core `ClearableNumberField`, so clearing genuinely means "use the default" - 100% opacity / 16px padding.) (**Admin tabs now sign themselves out.** A tab left open past the 24-hour session limit kept showing the last-rendered admin screen until the next request bounced it. New `components/admin/SessionExpiryWatcher.tsx`, mounted by `AdminShell`, warns in a corner banner 2 minutes out and then goes to `/<adminPath>/login?next=…&expired=1`, where `LoginForm` explains why. Fed by `sessionExpiresInMs` from the admin layout: `validateSessionWithMeta`/`getSessionWithMeta` now return `{ user, expiresAt }` and `getSessionFromCookie` derives from the same cached lookup, so no extra query. Pure clock arithmetic client-side - no polling, no requests.) (**Product 3D views: thumbnails were frozen, brightness parity, and idle motion is now a single nudge by default.** `tick()` in `lib/three/thumb-stage.ts` scheduled its next frame on `spin > 0`, and `spin` is 0 on the first frame of every run (no previous timestamp for the delta), so the strip drew one still picture and never rotated again on any site - it now continues on the settings intent rather than the computed step. The same renderer never had `toneMapping`/`toneMappingExposure` set either, so the strip drew at three's defaults while the stage drew through the owner's tone curve - also fixed. New settings `autoRotateStyle` (`'continuous'` default, unchanged behaviour | `'nudge'`) and `autoRotateSweep` (degrees, default 40): `'nudge'` turns the model once through the sweep, eased over 1.6s, the first time it is on screen and then holds still. `autoRotateSpeed` applies to `'continuous'` only. Both styles now stop entirely while unseen - the stage parks its rAF loop on an `IntersectionObserver` when scrolled out of view, and a backgrounded tab was already free.) (**Backup round-trip test moved off Neon onto the self-hosted OVH Postgres VPS.** No Neon API key exists any more, so `lib/backup/neon-branch.ts` is gone and `lib/backup/vps-database.ts` replaces it: provisioning happens over SSH (`sshpass`, `OVH_SERVER`/`OVH_USER`/`OVH_PASSWORD` from root `.env`) as the `postgres` superuser, creating a throwaway login role and two throwaway databases; the destination is a `CREATE DATABASE ... TEMPLATE` clone of the seeded source in place of a Neon branch. Every created object is prefixed `cactus_rt_`, and the helper refuses to drop anything not matching that prefix, so the live `neondb` on the same server is never touched. Cleanup is unconditional - `afterAll` drops both databases and the role, plus a prefix-scoped sweep before and after every run - and was verified against the server afterwards: only `neondb`, `postgres`, `template0`, `template1` remain and no `cactus_rt%` role. All three round-trip cases pass on Postgres 18.) (**Twilio v0.1.21: routing-region field-name fix.** `getNumberRegion`/`setNumberRegion` in `lib/twilio.ts` read `voice_region`/`messaging_region` off the Routes v3 API response, which is always `undefined` - that API replies camelCase (`voiceRegion`/`messagingRegion`), unlike the classic 2010-04-01 API. Every live routing read misread as blank and fell back to the us1 default, so the admin country dropdown looked stuck on United States even when Twilio had the number on ie1/au1, and a successful `setNumberRegion` call threw a false "kept this number on United States" error because the verify-check misread its own POST response. Fixed by reading the camelCase fields; no schema/route/env change.) (**Twilio v0.1.20: uploaded greeting audio.** Each spoken slot (call greeting, voicemail greeting, closed voicemail greeting) can carry an uploaded MP3/WAV played with `<Play>` instead of the `<Say>` text/voice. Files land in the core media library's root `twilio` folder on the active media provider (B2 on deskwell) via new `admin/greeting-audio` (POST multipart, `twilio.manage`, `validateNonImageUpload`, normalised to `audio/mpeg`/`audio/wav`, 10 MB cap, gemini-style folder-ensure with create-race handling); the rule stores only the media id (migration `007_greeting_audio.sql`, three `*_audio_media_id` TEXT DEFAULT `''` columns, mirrored into `001_initial.sql`). Twilio and the admin's inline player fetch bytes through new public `public/audio/[mediaId]` (unauthenticated by design - callers hear it anyway - but 404s any id not referenced by a rule's audio columns, so it cannot proxy arbitrary media like digital products; reads by provider+key via `downloadMedia`, serves the Media row's mimeType, `nosniff`, 5-min cache). The forwarding PUT validates submitted audio ids exist and are `audio/*` (same publish-hazard reasoning). Precedence in `voicemailGreetingTwiml` (new pure fn in `lib/voicemail.ts`, tested): closed audio > closed words > everyday audio > everyday words/stock line; call greeting: audio > text. `lib/greeting-audio.ts` (deliberately DB-free) holds types/limits/`greetingAudioUrl`. UI: `GreetingAudioControl` per slot (upload-on-choose, `pending` until the rule is saved since the public route only serves saved ids, then inline `<audio>` player + Remove); phone previews hidden while audio is set (they'd read words a real call wouldn't say). **BLOCKER: backup round-trip gate could not run - `NEON_API_KEY` left `.env` with the OVH migration (2026-07-20); suite fails on the missing key. Schema-coverage backstop passes (TEXT columns). Needs a Neon key before release.**) (**Twilio v0.1.19: Generative voices are us1-only - an ie1 call asking for one dies with Twilio 13520 "Say: Invalid text".** Live case (deskwell, ie1-homed account): webhook correctly set on the ie1 resource, every inbound call reached the site and got well-formed TwiML back, then died after ~3s on `<Say voice="Polly.Amy-Generative">` - Twilio's debugger logged 13520 per call. Twilio's docs nowhere state the restriction; proven empirically via the ie1 Calls/Events + Alerts APIs (same TwiML worked when the number was us1-routed). Fix: `lib/voices.ts` marks the three Generative voices `usOnly` with a `regionalFallback` (their Neural sibling) and exports `voiceAvailableInRegion`/`voiceForRegion`; every render path - voice webhook, voicemail webhook take-message stage, greeting-preview - resolves the number's Region and swaps a us-only voice for its fallback rather than killing the call ('' / Twilio default is the last resort). `admin/numbers` now returns each number's `region` (null on lookup failure); `VoicePicker` takes it, disables us-only voices on non-us1 numbers with a "United States numbers only" suffix, and when the saved voice is one of them shows a note naming the voice callers actually hear. Settings tab credentials card reworked into numbered setup steps (country first, then SID + Primary auth token off the API keys & tokens page, SK-key warning); forwarding card intro now says saving wires Twilio automatically and explains the console's per-country settings copies (the wrong country's page looks empty). `lib/voices.test.ts` added (9 tests incl. every usOnly voice has a valid region-safe fallback). Module 0.1.19 in both manifests, not yet released.) (**Twilio v0.1.18: a routing change was never verified against Twilio's own response.** `setNumberRegion` POSTed the Routes API and, on any 200, blindly trusted the request had taken - `setSiteNumberRegion` then wrote the requested region to `tw_site_numbers` unconditionally. Live case (deskwell): the Country dropdown kept reverting to United States after 5+ minutes with no error anywhere, on an account whose Routes API is otherwise reachable and correctly credentialed - consistent with Twilio accepting the POST syntactically while declining to actually move the number (some account/number combinations aren't eligible) and just echoing the unchanged Region back. `setNumberRegion` now reads `voice_region` back off the POST response and throws if it doesn't match what was requested, naming the Region Twilio actually kept - turning a silent, indefinitely-repeating revert into a real error the admin can act on or take to Twilio support.) (**Twilio v0.1.17: voice webhook is per-Region - a routed number was never getting one.** Twilio's own docs, quoted verbatim: "Your phone number's webhook configuration is Region-specific and may vary between different Regions," with the advice to check the target Region's `IncomingPhoneNumbers` resource before routing there. `setNumberVoiceUrl` previously always wrote to the home Region (comment wrongly called it "account-level") - so a number routed to `ie1` had forwarding/voicemail configured only on its `us1` resource, which Twilio never looks at once the number is actually processed in Ireland: calls simply went unanswered with nothing on the site's side showing wrong (live case - deskwell, UK number routed to `ie1`, "Ireland config not set up to send calls to our site" in the Twilio console). `setNumberVoiceUrl` now takes a `region` param; the forwarding route (`app/api/admin/twilio/forwarding/route.ts`) resolves it via `resolveNumberRegion` before every save. `setSiteNumberRegion` (`lib/numbers.ts`) also now re-applies the existing webhook to the NEW Region right after a country change, via the new `getRuleForNumber` export in `lib/forwarding.ts` - otherwise switching Country broke a number's forwarding all over again the moment the routing change landed, since the old Region kept the webhook and the new one had never been given one.) (**Twilio v0.1.16: region change no longer self-reverts + routing-read errors surfaced.** `syncSiteNumbers` now returns a per-SID Map of failed live routing reads instead of swallowing them; `mergedListing` attaches each as `routesError` on the listing entry and `TwilioSettingsTab` shows it as a per-number warning ("country shown is the last one saved here") - previously an erroring Routes lookup made a number look permanently "stuck" on its stored country with zero signal anywhere. Self-revert fix: the set-region action wrote the new region, then its response listing re-read live routing from the Routes API - which still reports the OLD region for up to five minutes after Twilio accepts a change - and `syncSiteNumbers` overwrote the just-saved value with that stale truth, so the Country dropdown silently snapped back with no error. `syncSiteNumbers` gains `opts.refreshRegions` (default true); the set-region response passes `false` and trusts stored values, the next ordinary listing re-syncs from Twilio once the change has bedded in.) (**Twilio v0.1.15: Routes API is us1-only - non-us1 homes skip per-number routing.** Live ie1-homed account (deskwell) proved `routes.dublin.ie1.twilio.com` answers 404 "Endpoint is not supported in realm 'ie1'": the Inbound Processing Region API exists at `routes.twilio.com` (us1) only and is a feature *for* us1-homed accounts. New `perNumberRoutingAvailable()` (`getHomeRegion() === 'us1'`) gates it: `getNumberRegion` returns home without calling, `setNumberRegion` throws plain English, `routesFetch` pins host+creds to us1. On a non-us1 home every number is processed at home, so `mapRow`/`resolveNumberRegion`/`getDefaultSmsNumber` override stored region with home (rows written while the site was set to United States said us1 and pointed log/SMS/recording queries at an empty region). Settings tab hides the per-number Country select and the Other-countries token fields when home ≠ us1.) (**Twilio v0.1.14: reject API-key SIDs with plain-English errors.** `accountSidProblem()` (exported, `lib/twilio.ts`) validates `TWILIO_ACCOUNT_SID` against `^AC[0-9a-f]{32}$` inside `regionCredentials` - an `SK…` API-key SID (the classic paste mistake, which previously produced a baffling 20404 `/Accounts/SK….json not found`) now throws a message explaining API keys are unusable here (webhook signatures are HMAC'd with the region's *auth token*, so an API key would silently break forwarding). `TwilioApiError` gains a 20404 hint; `TwilioSettingsTab` blocks saving an `SK…` value into the SID or any token field with the same explanation, and its intro copy now points at the console's "API keys & tokens" page / per-region Primary auth token.) (**Twilio v0.1.13: configurable account home region.** `TWILIO_HOME_REGION` env + account-country picker on the settings tab. The module no longer assumes a `us1`-homed account: `getHomeRegion()` (replaces the `HOME_REGION` const) drives the connection test, number listing and Routes API; `regionTokenEnvVar()` (replaces the static `REGION_TOKEN_ENV` map) puts the home region's token in the main `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN` and others in `TWILIO_AUTH_TOKEN_<REGION>` (added `_US1`). Failed REST calls throw a new `TwilioApiError` naming region/host/HTTP-status/Twilio-code, so a bare "Authenticate" (code 20003) now explains itself. Fixes an Ireland-homed account being rejected at `api.twilio.com`.) (**Core: pin shop v0.1.83, shop-variations v0.1.69 (v0.5.627).** `modules.json` pins bumped for the Tabs/Configure/scroll-spy and pinned-mobile-gallery fixes below.) (**Shop: Product Tabs - action (Add to cart / Configure) now leads the strip & flows with Tab alignment, strip opens on the action not Description, Configure lands on the product title (`#spd-top`); plus earlier padding fields, scroll-spy rewrite, mobile pinned-gallery stacking.** `Product: Tabs` block (`modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`) gains `padTop`/`padBottom` number fields (0-64, default 16); applied as `--spd-tabnav-pt`/`--spd-tabnav-pb` inline vars read by `.spd-tab-nav`'s padding. `ProductSectionTabs` (`modules/shop/components/public/ProductDetailIslands.tsx`) takes a `navStyle` prop; its scroll-spy dropped the IntersectionObserver band (previous section's tail kept the old tab highlighted after a jump) for a rAF scroll listener picking the last section whose top passed its own computed `scroll-margin-top`, with a bottom-of-page fallback to the last section. The action (Add to cart / Configure) now leads the strip - rendered first, filled; the `.spd-tab-action` `margin-inline-start:auto` was dropped so it flows with the block's Tab alignment instead of pinning to the far right. The strip also opens on it: `ProductSectionTabs` seeds `active` from a `leadAnchor` (`#spd-buy` when an action exists), which is also prepended to the scroll-spy targets, so at the top - buy area in view - the action reads as current and no section link (previously Description) lights up until the shopper scrolls into a section. The Configure click now prefers `document.getElementById('spd-top')` - the product name; `ShopDetailTitleRsc`'s `<h1>` gains `id="spd-top"` + the sections' `scroll-margin-top` so the title isn't scrolled under the header/tab bar - then `document.querySelector('[data-spd-configure]')` (documented provider hook), then the `#spd-buy` href (no-JS fallback). shop-variations marks both its options areas (`VariantParts.tsx` granular part, `DetailSlotPartsClient.tsx` inline slot area) with `data-spd-configure` + a scroll margin. Mobile pinned gallery (`modules/shop-variations`): `.svr-mstick` strip now pins at `calc(--spd-header-h + --spd-tabnav-h)` so a sticky tab bar stays visible above it; the `.svr-gallery-pinned .spd-tab-nav.sticky{visibility:hidden}` rule replaced with `z-index:31`; `use-sticky-mobile-gallery.ts` thresholds add `tabNavH()`. No schema change.) (**Header: SiteLogo no longer flashes oversized on first mobile load.** The logo `<img>` (`SiteLogoRsc` in `lib/puck/config.tsx`, mirrored in `lib/puck/components/SiteLogoClient.tsx`) dropped its unconditional inline `transition:height 0.25s ease`. That transition animated the initial responsive height resolution: on an uncached load the inline desktop base (`--header-cell-height`) could paint before the in-body `<style>` mobile media rule applied, and the armed transition then animated big->correct, so the logo loaded oversized then shrank. The transition is now emitted via `<style>` scoped to `header[data-shrink-ready] img[data-site-logo]`; `HeaderShrinkScroll` (`lib/puck/components/HeaderShrinkScroll.tsx`) sets `data-shrink-ready` on the header in a `requestAnimationFrame` after its first `apply()` (past first paint), so the initial breakpoint/shrink resolution never animates and only scroll-driven shrink does. No schema/API change. **Core: pin shop-variations v0.1.67 (v0.5.624).** `modules.json` shop-variations pin bumped to `v0.1.67` for the accordion fix below. **Shop: Variant Options accordion hides the toggle for single-value sections.** `VariantOptionsAccordion` (`modules/shop-variations/components/public/VariantParts.tsx`) now computes `availableCount = option.values.filter((v) => sel.isAvailable(option.id, v.id)).length` per section; `collapsible = availableCount > 1`. When a section has one or no reachable value (its single value is already auto-picked by `withAutoSelected`) it renders a static `<div>` header (option name + chosen label, no chevron, no `onClick`, no `aria-expanded`) instead of the toggle `<button>`, and is forced closed (`open = collapsible && openIds.has(...)`). An upstream change that widens it past one value restores the normal openable button. Header markup factored into a shared `headerStyle`/`headerInner`. No schema change. **Core: pin shop v0.1.81 (v0.5.623).** `modules.json` shop pin bumped to `v0.1.81` for the Tabs-strip action-CTA + sticky fixes below. **Shop: Product: Tabs strip gains a trailing action CTA + sticky fixes.** `ProductSectionTabs` (`modules/shop/components/public/ProductDetailIslands.tsx`) takes a new optional `action` prop (`TabAction` = `{kind:'add',productId,label}` | `{kind:'configure',anchor,label}`); it renders a filled `.spd-tab-btn.spd-tab-action` pill at the end of the strip - a `<button>` that calls `addToCart(productId,1)` (no-options products) or an `<a href="#spd-buy">` jump (products with options). `ShopDetailTabsRsc` computes it: `hasOptions = ctx.slot?.PurchaseArea || ctx.slot.covered.includes('PurchaseArea')` → Configure; else Add to cart (omitted when `ctx.outOfStock`). The Add to Cart part (`ShopDetailAddToCart`/`Rsc`) now wraps its output in `<div id="spd-buy" class="spd-buy-anchor">` (jump target; `scroll-margin-top` clears the header). Sticky nav (`.spd-tab-nav.sticky`) now pins flush at `top:var(--spd-header-h)` (was `+8px`, which left a see-through band); the client island publishes its measured height as `--spd-tabnav-h` on the root while sticky, and `.spd-section`/`.spd-acc` scroll-margin now adds it so jump-links clear the pinned strip. Editor preview `ShopDetailTabs` appends a static "Add to cart" span for parity. No schema change. **Shop: Product: Tabs becomes nav-only and jumps to Product: Sections (shop v0.1.80).** `ShopDetailTabs`/`ShopDetailTabsRsc` (`modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`) no longer render any section content - the block is a navigation strip only. RSC builds a `{label, anchor}[]` from the shared `buildDetailSections(ctx)` and delegates to the renamed client island `ProductSectionTabs` (`modules/shop/components/public/ProductDetailIslands.tsx`, was `ProductTabs`), which renders `<nav class="spd-tab-nav">` of `<a href="#spd-sec-…">` pill links (no `.spd-tabs` wrapper, so a `position:sticky` nav can travel past the sibling Sections block instead of being trapped in a wrapper only as tall as itself) plus an `IntersectionObserver` scroll-spy that toggles `.on`/`aria-current` on the link whose section is nearest the top. The old self-contained `.spd-panel` markup + CSS rule are removed. `navClassFor` gains a `divider` bool and now emits a `.spd-tab-nav.divider` class (CSS added); the editor preview `ShopDetailTabs` mirrors the island markup (span vs `<a>`). `.spd-section` lost its `max-width:900px` and `.spd-tabs p` its `max-width:70ch`, so Product: Sections fills its container. All three product-detail starters (`lib/starterLayouts.ts` Default/Editorial/Compact) now ship a `ShopDetailSections` block (`display:stacked, divider:no`) beside each `ShopDetailTabs` so the nav always has section anchors to target. No schema change. Module bumped 0.1.79 → 0.1.80 (`cactus.module.json` + `package.json`), pin updated in root `modules.json`. **Shop: Variant Options block gains accordion layout + swatch-only choices (shop-variations v0.1.66).** `shopVariantOptionsPuckComponent` (`modules/shop-variations/components/puck/variant-parts.tsx`) gets four new radio fields on top of the existing `labelPlacement`: `displayMode` (`inline` default / `accordion`), `accordionInitial` (`closed` default / `first` / `all`), `accordionOnSelect` (`none` / `openNext` default / `openNextCloseCurrent`), `swatchDisplay` (`pill` default / `swatchOnly`). A per-block `resolveFields` hides `accordionInitial`/`accordionOnSelect` unless `displayMode === 'accordion'`, hides `labelPlacement` in accordion mode (the section heading is the name), and hides `accordionOnSelect` when `accordionInitial === 'all'` (nothing left to auto-open) - shown for both `closed` and `first`. Render lives in `VariantOptionsPart` (`components/public/VariantParts.tsx`): accordion mode delegates to new client component `VariantOptionsAccordion` (per-option collapsible; open state seeded from `accordionInitial`, deferred `pending`→effect opens/closes the next section on choice via `OptionControl`'s new `onChoose` callback). `OptionControl` gains `hideLabel` (accordion panels), `swatchDisplay`, and `onChoose` props; swatch-only renders a bare colour dot / 28px thumbnail wrapped in new `ValueTooltip` (hover chip matching core `.theme-toggle-tip`), name carried on `title`/`aria-label` for a11y. Props threaded through `shopVariantOptionsPuckRscComponent` (`variant-parts.rsc.tsx`). No schema change. Module bumped 0.1.65 → 0.1.66 (`cactus.module.json` + `package.json`), pin updated in root `modules.json`. **Product: Tabs and Product: Sections split into two blocks (shop, working tree, unreleased, v0.1.79).** The combined `ShopDetailTabs` block (`modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`, was labelled "Product: Tabs / Sections") is split in two: `ShopDetailTabs` ("Product: Tabs") drops the `display` field entirely and always renders the tab-bar mode, keeping only `align`/`sticky`/`divider`; a new `ShopDetailSections` block ("Product: Sections", `shopDetailSectionsPuckComponent`/`shopDetailSectionsPuckRscComponent`) takes over the "Section display" field, now `stacked`/`accordion` only (no `tabs` option, since that's the Tabs block's job) plus its own `divider`. Both still build their section list from the one shared `buildDetailSections(ctx)` helper and share `tabsCss`/`sectionAnchorId`, so the standalone "Product: Section links" block (`ShopDetailSectionNav`) now pairs with Sections (not Tabs) for its stacked/accordion jump-link targets. Registered in `cactus.module.json` (`puckBlocks` array) + `inject-part-context.ts` `DETAIL_PART_TYPES`. **Deliberately no back-compat**: per this being a fresh-install-only platform, the old combined block's `display: stacked|accordion` behaviour is gone outright rather than migrated - any already-saved layout using that mode on `ShopDetailTabs` will render tabs-only until an editor swaps in the new Sections block by hand. Shop module version bumped 0.1.78 → 0.1.79 (`cactus.module.json` + `package.json`). **Product Detail tabs gain stacked/accordion display, sticky + alignment, and a standalone "Section links" block (shop, working tree, unreleased, v0.1.77).** The `ShopDetailTabs` block (`modules/shop/components/puck/parts/detail-parts.tsx`, relabelled "Product: Tabs / Sections") gets four fields: `display` (tabs default / stacked / accordion), `align` (left/centre/right, tabs mode), `sticky` (tabs mode), `divider` (top rule+gap, default on - turning it off fixes the stray white space when the block is dragged to the top of the page, since the 40px margin is now the opt-in `.spd-tabs.divider` class). Stacked and accordion are pure RSC (no client island; accordion is native `<details>`, first section open); each section carries an anchor id `spd-sec-<id>`. New block **`ShopDetailSectionNav`** ("Product: Section links") renders the same nav strip on its own as `<a href="#spd-sec-…">` jump links, so admins can place the links above the image while the sections stay below - pair it with a stacked/accordion Tabs block. Both blocks build their section list from one shared `buildDetailSections(ctx)` helper so links can't point at a missing section. `ProductTabs` island (`ProductDetailIslands.tsx`) gained `align`/`sticky`/`divider` props. Registered in `cactus.module.json` + `inject-part-context.ts` `DETAIL_PART_TYPES`. No schema change. **Google Sheet Pull preview now sees provider columns + Push overwrite guard (google-sheet-products-for-shop + shop-variations + product-attributes-for-shop + product-3d-views-for-shop, working tree, unreleased).** Editing a **3D Files** or **attribute** cell used to preview "0 to update" then apply the change anyway - the preview only diffed the seven built-in variant columns. Added an optional read-only `rowChanged` to the `variant-field-provider` contract, implemented in both provider modules (3D via a shared `planRow`; attributes via a new non-creating `findAttributeValueByLabel`), and called from `predictVariations` in the module's `lib/preview.ts`. Separately, **Push** now refuses to overwrite a sheet edited since the last sync: it reads the sheet's Drive `modifiedTime` (`getSheetModifiedTime`) and 409s with `needsConfirm` unless `{force:true}`, which the toolbar turns into a `confirm()`. No schema change. Full detail in the module sections below.) (**3D model optimisation, KTX2 textures, parallel model fetch (core + product-3d-views-for-shop, working tree, unreleased).** GLB models are now compressed server-side through the media library's existing in-place optimise: new `lib/media/model-optimise.ts` (gltf-transform + meshoptimizer + draco3d, all visually-lossless settings), wired into `optimiseMediaInPlace` and written back over the model's **own storage key** so `p3d_models` rows are never stranded. New uploads optimise automatically via `autoOptimiseNewUpload`; older files get the library's existing ⚡/Optimise/bulk controls, because eligibility collapsed onto one shared `isOptimisableType` with a test asserting the Prisma clause agrees with it. Viewer side: `KHR_texture_basisu` decodes at last (transcoder vendored beside Draco, both now served by one `/decoders` route, old `/draco` kept as a deprecated alias), and `parseRaw` starts the model download **before** awaiting its loader imports instead of after. Full detail in Media Layer and the module's section.) (**3D viewer: Draco, on-demand rendering, context-loss recovery, keyboard control (product-3d-views-for-shop, v0.1.57).** `KHR_draco_mesh_compression` now decodes - the decoder is committed under the module's `assets/draco` and served by a new public `GET /api/m/product-3d-views-for-shop/draco/[file]`, the first user of core's generic `modules/*/assets/**` tracing entry, and core's CSP gained `worker-src 'self' blob:` because three builds the decoder into a Blob-URL Worker. Both the stage viewer and the thumbnail strip now draw only when something has actually changed rather than 60fps into a still picture. Both recover from a lost WebGL context by rebuilding (the stage onto a fresh canvas keyed on a `generation` state, the strip by replacing the shared renderer and re-pointing every scene at its environment via the new `applyEnvironment`). The stage canvas is focusable and driven by arrow keys, `+`/`-` and `Home`, with the drag-versus-keys hint chosen by CSS `:focus-visible` rather than React `onFocus`. Full detail in the module's section.) (**Parallel bulk image jobs (core).** Bulk optimise / change-ratio / resize no longer hand the whole selection to one request that re-encodes it end to end. New `app/cactus-admin/media/bulkImageJob.ts` (`runBulkImageJob(endpoint, ids, body, {changedKey, onProgress})`, `BULK_CONCURRENCY = 6`) drains the selection through 6 concurrent workers, each POSTing an existing bulk route with a **list of one**, so every image lands in its own serverless invocation: 6 sharp re-encodes at once, no request carrying more than one image's work (the 60s route ceiling stops being a cliff on big selections), and a live count. Server routes and their per-item tallies/naming are unchanged - the workers merge the tallies (`changed`/`optimised`, `skipped`, `failed`, `bytesSaved`). A 4xx other than 404 aborts the whole run and throws once (it would refuse every id identically); 5xx/network/404 counts as that one id failing. Callers: `MediaLibrary.optimiseBulk` (busy toast "Optimising 214/600…"), `MediaAspectDialog`/`MediaResizeDialog` bulk branches (button "Working… 12/60"); single-item paths still use the `[id]/*` routes. **Required companion fix:** `rewriteMediaReferencesInContent` (`lib/media/upload.ts`) was a read-modify-write - `findMany` every `InfoPage`/`Layout`, swap in node, write the whole JSON blob back - which was only safe because these jobs ran strictly serially; two images on the same page rewritten concurrently each read before the other wrote, so the second write restored the first's old url moments before its blob was deleted (verified on a throwaway Neon project: the swap really was lost). Now one atomic `UPDATE … SET col = replace(replace(col::text, urlFrom, urlTo), keyFrom, keyTo)::jsonb WHERE strpos(...) > 0` per table via new private `swapInBuilderJson(table, urlFrom, urlTo, keyFrom, keyTo)`; url swapped before key, as before. An empty needle means "that pair didn't move" (replace with `''` is identity, guarded in WHERE by `<> ''`); `strpos` not `LIKE` because filenames carry underscores; `replace()` on NULL yields NULL so `publishedData` needs no special case. Also removes a per-image full read of every page's builder JSON, itself a large part of the slowness. Module rewriters (`core.media-reference-rewriters`) were already single atomic statements keyed on the exact old url, so they were safe as-is. Same day: **Bulk storage-check repairs (core).** Big storage-check clean-ups no longer time out: `purgeMissingRows` now reference-checks candidates in one pass via new `getMediaReferencesBulk(mediaIds)` in `lib/media/upload.ts` (grouped counts + one usage index, `getMediaReferences` delegates to it) and deletes rows with a single `deleteMany` instead of per-row queries; `MediaStorageCheck.tsx` sends `purge-missing` in batches of 200 and `delete-orphans` in batches of 25, each POST retried up to 3 times with backoff, non-JSON responses (gateway timeout pages, Safari's "The string did not match the expected pattern") turned into a plain-English error, running progress note during multi-batch runs. Same day: **Parallel media uploads (core).** `MediaLibrary.enqueueFiles` now answers every name-clash dialog up front (serial, file order - Cancel still means nothing was sent), then drains the batch through a pool of 6 concurrent workers (`CONCURRENT_UPLOADS`, matching the browser’s ~6-connections-per-host cap) instead of one file at a time; per-task progress unchanged, one slow file no longer blocks the rest. Earlier same-day: **Clearing entries whose file has gone (core).** The media Storage check's "Files that have gone" group gained a repair to match the other two: `purgeMissingRows` in `lib/media/reconcile.ts` behind `POST /api/admin/media/storage-check { action: 'purge-missing' }`, deleting the `Media` rows only - never a blob, because the object is already gone, and calling the provider would only raise a not-found. Covers the case where files are deleted in the provider's own console (Backblaze etc), which tells Cactus nothing. Referenced rows are skipped and listed back unless `force`, and `MediaStorageCheck.tsx` renders that list with a "Remove them anyway" button; its post-repair re-scan no longer wipes the sentence saying what the repair did (`scan(keepNote)`). Earlier same-tree work: **Folder-scoped media search + upload name prompts (core + product-3d-views-for-shop, working tree, unreleased).** Media-library search now reads the folder you are standing in (direct contents only) with an "In <folder>" / "Everywhere" scope select beside the box, a chip that says which, and a "Search all folders" button on the empty state; `searchEverywhere` state in `MediaLibrary.tsx` feeds `folderScope`, and `viewingAllFolders` replaced the scattered `browseAll || search || tagFilter` checks in the breadcrumb/tree/drop-label. Uploading a file whose name is already in the destination folder now asks (`UploadClashDialog`, new `POST /api/admin/media/name-check`): Replace routes to `replaceOneFile` so the existing row keeps its id/url, Keep both re-files the `File` under the server-suggested `name-1.ext`, Skip drops the one file, Cancel abandons the rest of the batch. `replaceOneFile` now resolves its content type with `uploadTypeForFile` like the upload path did, so a 3D model can take the direct route instead of dying on the serverless body cap. In the 3D module, `buildModelKey` only falls back to the nanoid form when there is no usable filename at all (a missing product slug now keeps the uploaded name instead of minting `t_nAo5Nr9-oblong-100cm.glb`), and returns `taken` when the preferred name is occupied; `models/upload-url` answers `{ clash }` and signs nothing until the editor replies `onClash: replace|suffix`, with `recordDirect` adopting the existing Media row via `adoptReplacementBlob` (and `ownsMedia: false`) when the bytes overwrote one. `useModelClashPrompt` is the shared dialog for both upload surfaces. Earlier same-tree work: **Google Sheet pull preview + auto-resume (google-sheet-products-for-shop, working tree, unreleased).** The pull preview's variations "to update" is now a real field diff (`variationRowChanged` in `lib/preview.ts`) instead of counting every matched combination, so Push→Pull with no edits previews 0 updates; the browser step loop auto-retries a failed/errored step (5 consecutive, 2-8s backoff, reset on progress) and reopening the modal onto an unfinished job auto-resumes - Continue is the last resort. See the module section. Earlier same-tree work: **Sourced swatch pictures stay with their attribute (product-attributes-for-shop + shop-variations, working tree, unreleased).** shop-variations' `fileSwatchImage` no-ops for values with a `source_ref`; product-attributes' refile pushes rewritten urls into `svr_option_values` via `syncSourcedOptionValues`; the option-source provider lists attributes in screen order and the picker merges repeated group headings (fixes the "three Dynamic groups" picker bug); new `POST admin/refile-swatches` + **Tidy picture folders** button repairs already-misfiled pictures. See the product-attributes module section. Also: **Prisma can no longer reach the browser bundle unnoticed (core + four modules, working tree, unreleased).** New `lib/db/client-bundle.test.ts` walks the real import graph from every `'use client'` file, following only value imports (`import type` and `import { type A }` are erased, so they are ignored), and fails if any of them can reach `lib/db/prisma`. It exists because v0.5.595 put `Prisma.defineExtension()` at module scope in `lib/db/prisma.ts`: that call throws in a browser, and because it fails at module-evaluation time it takes down the whole page rather than the one component that leaked. It turned four long-dormant leaks fatal at once. `product-3d-views-for-shop` (v0.1.52) value-imported `P3D_CONFIG_DEFAULTS` from its prisma-importing `lib/config`, which killed **/cactus-admin/config entirely** on a live site; fixed by splitting the schema/type/defaults/parser into `lib/config-shared.ts`. `shop` (v0.1.75) did the same with `DEFAULT_BREAKPOINTS` from `lib/breakpoints` (prisma via `lib/config/site`) in `parts/detail-parts` + `parts/card-parts`, which back 16 Puck blocks and land in the page builder's client bundle - split into `lib/breakpoints-shared.ts`. `boards` (v0.1.11, 1 block), `directory` (v0.1.11, 7 blocks) and `gazette` (v0.1.11, 9 blocks) had Puck blocks declaring `rscComponent` with no `rscImport`, so one file held both the editor preview and the prisma-backed render and the editor registry imported the lot; each is now an editor half plus a `.rsc` half with `rscImport` declared, matching the split shop and boards' other blocks already used. **The rule this encodes:** a Puck block's editor component and its RSC render must live in separate files whenever the render touches the database, and a client component may only ever `import type` from a module that reaches prisma. Neither tsc, eslint nor the build catches a breach - only this test does. Also: **Suppliers are a directory, not just a name on a product (shop + shop-variations, working tree, unreleased).** Shop settings' "Add supplier name to product" is now "Enable suppliers support", and switching it on adds a **Suppliers** entry to the Shop sidebar group plus a Suppliers admin screen. New shop migration `007_suppliers.sql` creates `shp_suppliers` (name, account number, discount %, ENABLED/DISABLED status, contact name/phone/email/address, notes) and indexes `shp_products.supplier`. Products link to a supplier **by name**, not by id: the existing `shp_products.supplier` text column from `006` is unchanged, so the CSV columns, the import engine and every supplier already typed by hand keep working untouched - and a rename moves the products with it (`renameSupplier`, one transaction). The product editor's Details tab and shop-variations' grid column both became dropdowns fed by `GET admin/suppliers?for=picker` (enabled suppliers only), each with an "Add a new …" option that POSTs a new record without leaving the product, and each keeping a value that is no longer offered as an option of its own so opening a product can never silently blank it. The sidebar link is conditional, which core's manifest-driven sidebar has no mechanism for, so the shop module patches its own stored `Module.manifest.navEntries` (`lib/supplier-nav.ts`); because a module update rewrites that stored manifest from file, the sync is also called from the settings GET and the dashboard-widget GET so the link heals itself rather than needing the setting toggled again. Also: **The media library can be reconciled against storage (core, working tree, unreleased).** New `lib/media/reconcile.ts` + `GET/POST /api/admin/media/storage-check` + `MediaStorageCheck.tsx` under the library page report objects with no `Media` row ("leftovers"), rows whose object has gone, and rows whose `sizeBytes` disagrees with the object - and repair the last two categories. `lib/media/upload.ts` gains the read-only primitives behind it: `headMediaSize`, `listStoredMediaKeys` (S3 family / Vercel Blob / Supabase; `null` = "cannot tell" for Cloudinary+ImageKit, deliberately never an empty list), `mediaKeyPrefix`, and `confirmedSizeBytes`, which closes the hole that made a wrong size possible: the direct-upload paths (`/record`, `[id]/replace`) recorded the browser's `file.size` on trust, having never seen the bytes. Also: **Products and variations can record a supplier (shop + shop-variations, working tree, unreleased).** New shop migration `006_supplier.sql` adds a nullable `supplier` TEXT column to `shp_products`, carried on `ShpProduct`, `CreateProductInput`/`UpdateProductInput` (both raw column lists in `createProduct` and `duplicateProduct` included), the admin POST/PUT bodies, the product CSV (`supplier`, listed in `OPTIONAL_CSV_COLUMNS` so older exports still import) and the import engine. Five `ShpConfig` keys behind it: `supplierFieldEnabled`, `supplierLabelPreset`, `supplierLabelCustom`, `supplierShowOnFrontend`, `supplierFieldScope`. Variations reuse the same column, since a variation is a hidden child `shp_products` row - shop-variations gains a grid column, a `supplier` field on its PATCH body, `VariantEditorRow`/`ChildProductFields`/`ChildEditRow` and its own CSV `Supplier` column, all gated on scope = PRODUCTS_AND_VARIATIONS. Storefront rendering is a Specification-tab row on the product detail page, gated on both switches, and it does swap per chosen variation: shop's `lib/detail-slot.ts` gained a fourth slot, `SupplierValue` (`ShopDetailSlotName`/`ShopDetailPartsProvider`/`ShopDetailSlot`), narrower than Gallery/Price/PurchaseArea - shop still renders the row's label and table markup itself, the slot only supplies the value cell, so there is no `coveredSlots` case for it. shop-variations implements it (`VariantSlotSupplierValue` in `components/public/DetailSlotParts.tsx` / `DetailSlotPartsClient.tsx`, registered in `lib/detail-parts-provider.ts`) by reading `sel.variant?.supplier` off the same `useVariationSelection` store Price/Gallery/PurchaseArea already use, falling back to the parent's supplier (the `fallback` prop) until a variant with its own is chosen. `VariantSelectorPayload`'s `sku`-shaped `supplier` field on `VariantSelectorVariant` is deliberately gated server-side in `getVariantSelectorPayload` (`exposeSupplier` - only populated when `supplierFieldEnabled && supplierShowOnFrontend && supplierFieldScope === 'PRODUCTS_AND_VARIATIONS'`), so a supplier kept as a private admin reference is never present in the public payload even though the query column is always fetched. See the `ShpConfig` entry and the shop/shop-variations sections.) (**Weight-based shipping is now a switch (shop v0.1.71 + shop-variations v0.1.58, unreleased).** New `weightBasedShippingEnabled` config key, default true, surfaced as a "Charge postage by weight" card at the top of Shop → Tax & shipping. (**The media library's Unused and Optimisable tiles now tell the truth (working tree, core + 8 modules, unreleased).** New `core.media-usage-providers` extension point (`lib/media/usage-providers.ts`) lets a module hand core the media references held in its own tables; shop, shop-variations, product-attributes-for-shop, product-3d-views-for-shop, product-downloads-for-shop, boards, directory and gazette each register one, so product photos, swatches, 3D models, downloads, board icons, directory galleries and article heroes stop being counted as **unused** and offered for bulk deletion. A provider that throws marks the index `degraded` and everything reads as in use. The Optimisable tile's drill-down gained a real `optimisable=1` filter matching the predicate the tile counts, instead of falling back to "all images". See the media API + usage index entries and each module section.) (**The per-option Refresh button is gone from the Variations tab (shop-variations v0.1.56).** It re-read a sourced option's attribute for new/renamed values on demand; `Add from a source` already covers picking up new values, and rename propagation already happens on its own, so the button added nothing worth the click. `refreshOption` and its handler are removed from `VariationsPanel.tsx`; the `POST /api/m/shop-variations/admin/options/[id]/refresh` route is untouched but now unreached from the admin UI.) (**Variation options come from attributes only, and new values go back (shop-variations v0.1.55 + product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.15).** The typed-in "Add an option" form is gone from the Variations tab - `Add from attributes` is the only way to make one - and a value typed into a sourced option's Add-value box is written to the attribute behind it first, through a new optional `createValue` on the `shop-variations.option-source` contract, then copied down carrying the source's ref. A source that refuses is a hard 400, not a quiet local write. See both module sections.) (**A picture swatch carries its own real-world size (working tree, product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.14 + product-3d-views-for-shop v0.1.49, unreleased).** `pat_attribute_values.swatch_size` (`007_swatch_size.sql`) is set beside the picture on the Attributes screen and stays editable afterwards. The material configurator's per-part **Size from** dropdown is gone with it - a part's scale now comes from the swatch it is painted with - and **Colour from** offers picture-swatch attributes and a fixed colour only, since nothing else carries both the picture and its size. Configs saved before this keep resolving off their stored size fields. See both module sections.) (**The 3D material configurator points at a helping, not an attribute (working tree, product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** Its **Overall height from**, **Colour from** and **Size from** dropdowns now list a repeated attribute once per helping, under that helping's name, and the resolver reads the value ticked under that helping rather than whichever row came back first. Per-product lists, an `assignment_id` on the child's values, and a bare attribute id kept as the stored id wherever there is nothing to tell apart - so nothing saved before this needs migrating. See the module section.) (**One attribute can be several variations columns on one product (working tree, product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.13, unreleased).** 005 let a product hold an attribute twice, but only for its own product-level ticks: the variations column list de-duplicated on attribute id and a per-variant write cleared every value of that attribute on that variant, so two helpings collapsed into one column and one answer was lost - hence the rule 005 shipped with, that a repeated attribute could not also be per-variant. The column is now keyed by **assignment**, `006_variation_columns_per_helping.sql` stamps `assignment_id` onto the per-variant rows 005 left NULL (no DDL; skipped when shop-variations is absent), and that rule is gone. A boardroom table can now carry "Main finish" and "Edge finish" off one Finish vocabulary, each set per variant. See the module section.) (**One product can use the same attribute more than once, and variants carry every price type (working tree, product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.11 + shop-variations v0.1.52, unreleased).** `pat_product_attributes` and `pat_product_values` both swap their composite primary keys for surrogate ids (`005_repeatable_product_attributes.sql`); a helping gains `name_override` and a tick gains `assignment_id`, so "Top material: Oak" and "Frame material: Steel" can sit on one product off one Material attribute. All but one helping of an attribute must be renamed - `UNIQUE NULLS NOT DISTINCT` enforces it, the editor and the PUT both say so first. Separately, the Variations grid now offers a column per price type switched on under Shop settings (was: the mandatory price only), and the storefront runs a variant's price through shop's `effectivePrice` so a variant on offer is charged and shown at its sale price. See both module sections.) (**Stale pooled query plans are cleared after a schema change (working tree, unreleased).** A schema change applied on Neon's direct endpoint leaves pgBouncer's own long-lived server connections holding query plans built against the old table shapes, so afterwards a request 500s or succeeds depending purely on which pooled connection it lands on (`cached plan must not change result type`, SQLSTATE 0A000). New `scripts/flush-pooled-plans.mjs` runs last in `build-migrate.mjs` and ends idle backends so the plans are rebuilt. This is what took every dwoffice.furniture product page down after v0.5.578. See the scripts section.) (**The same attribute can be added to one product as several options (working tree, shop-variations v0.1.50, unreleased).** Nothing keyed on a per-product source ref, so the only blocker was the option-name rule - now enforced on create (`POST admin/products/[id]/options` trims and 409s on a case-insensitive duplicate; it was unchecked before) and made workable in the picker: sources already on the product are badged with the names they use, the name box starts empty when the source's own name is taken, and Add stays disabled while the typed name clashes. New `svr_options.name_overridden` (`005_option_name_overridden.sql`) records a deliberately chosen name, set on create when it differs from the source's and on every rename, so a refresh stops reporting `nameDiffers` for it. See the shop-variations section.) (**Variation options can be built from an attribute, and refreshed from it later (working tree, shop-variations v0.1.49 + product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.9, unreleased).** New `shop-variations.option-source` extension point: a module offers ready-made option lists as plain data, shop-variations owns the picker (pick a source, tick which values, override the option name). Options remember `source_provider`/`source_ref` and values `source_ref` (`004_option_source.sql`), so a Refresh re-reads the source - adding and renaming only, never deleting, since every value has real variants hanging off it. See the shop-variations section.) (**The product CSV format carries every owner-editable field, and the Google Sheet gets real numbers (working tree, shop + google-sheet-products-for-shop, unreleased).** `CSV_COLUMNS` went 24 -> 39 (slug, dimensions, download rules, pre-order, related/upsell), row-building moved into shared `modules/shop/lib/csv-rows.ts`, the importer now leaves absent columns alone rather than blanking them, and the sheet writes numeric/boolean cells as numbers and booleans instead of text - see the Google Sheet Products for Shop section.) (**Product attribute names are unique per group rather than shop-wide (pin product-attributes-for-shop v0.1.8).** The duplicate guard ignored folders, so "Size" could exist once in the whole shop; it now scopes to the attribute's group (ungrouped counting as one), the PATCH route checks a group *move* as well as a rename, and the Add form gained a group picker. No schema change - see the product-attributes-for-shop section.) (**A module being updated no longer disappears from the site (working tree, core + shop + contact-form + ultimate-seo + shop-variations, unreleased).** The module status filter was hand-copied to 21 call sites and excluded `deploying`/`pending_deploy`, so updating any module silently removed everything it contributed - reported as 3D models vanishing on redeploy. Now centralised in `lib/modules/live-status.ts` with a test that fails on any reintroduced copy; see the Modules section.) (**Media-library uploads keep their filename in storage** - `buildLibraryUploadKey` files them as `<filename>.<ext>`, deduping `-2`/`-3` … against existing keys instead of hiding every object behind a nanoid prefix; `uploadMedia` gained a `presetKey` argument so the key the collision check chose is the key actually written. **3D models are named after their product, and can be uploaded from the media page (working tree, core + product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** Model keys were `<nanoid>-<filename>.glb`, so only the folder said which product a file belonged to; `lib/model-key.ts` now files them as `<parent-product-slug>-<filename>` via core's `exactName` flag, the way the shop already names product images, with a `-2`/`-3` suffix where a name is taken (exact-name keys overwrite, and two variations sharing an object is a deletion hazard). Separately, the media library itself refused every `.glb` as "not a supported image": `lib/media/limits.ts` gains `uploadTypeForFile` (models are typed from their **extension** - browsers report `.glb` as octet-stream), `isUploadableType` and `isDirectUploadType`, wired through the picker, preflight, `upload-client.ts`, `/upload-url` and `/record`. `ACCEPTED_UPLOAD_TYPES` stays image-only on purpose - it gates Replace and the image tools. The picker fix reached only the header Upload button: the empty-state and whitespace-menu input kept a hand-written image-only `accept`, so an empty folder - where a first model gets uploaded - greyed `.glb` out in the file explorer with no error. Both now take `UPLOAD_ACCEPT_ATTR` from `lib/media/limits.ts` (`IMAGE_ACCEPT_ATTR` for Replace, image-only by intent), a test in `model-types.test.ts` fails on any rehardcoded `accept`, and the whole media page is a drop target rather than the grid panel alone. See the Media Layer and Product 3D Views sections.) (**Product attributes can be filed into groups (working tree, product-attributes-for-shop 0.1.7, unreleased).** New `pat_attribute_groups` table + nullable `pat_attributes.group_id` (ON DELETE SET NULL) in `004_attribute_groups.sql`, CRUD at `admin/groups[/id]`, and a grouped attributes screen. Grouping is admin-only - no public read touched. The media folder path gains an optional group segment, so `refileAttributeSwatches` moves an attribute's **picture swatches** whenever it changes group, its group is renamed or deleted, or the attribute itself is renamed. Groups and attributes also gained **up/down ordering** (`admin/attributes/reorder`, `admin/groups/reorder`, whole-list writes), attribute order being the storefront filter order. See the Product Attributes section.) (**3D models are no longer served to anyone holding the url (working tree, core + product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** The media Worker's GET path now requires a signed `?t=` token for model extensions only (`lib/media/asset-token.ts` + `refuseUnauthorisedRead` in `workers/media-worker/index.ts`); the expiry is rounded up to a 24h bucket so every render emits the same url and browser/edge caching is untouched. Signed on the way out at five emit points, never stored. Fails open until an admin redeploys the Worker. See the media Worker section.) (**A variant holds a whole set of images, not one (working tree, shop-variations, unreleased).** The storage was always one-to-many (`shp_product_media` rows on the hidden child), but every read collapsed it with `SELECT DISTINCT ON (product_id)` and the picker threw away all but `items[0]`. Both `getVariantSelectorPayload` and `getEditorPayload` now read every `IMAGE` row ordered `is_primary DESC, position ASC` into `imageUrls: string[]` (replacing `imageUrl`), `PATCH admin/variants/[id]` takes `imageUrls`, the grid's `ImageCell` shows the first with a **+N** badge and *adds* on each pick rather than replacing, and both galleries (`VariantParts`, `DetailSlotPartsClient`) put the whole set at the front of the thumbnail strip via the hook's new `sel.variantImages`. No schema change.) (**The product image picker pages and sorts (shop v0.1.66).** `MediaPickerModal` no longer stops dead at the first 50 images: a **Load more** button appends the next page off core's existing `page`/`hasMore` support, and a sort dropdown (newest/oldest/name A-Z/Z-A) passes core's existing `sort` param - module-only change, no core diff - see shop's "Picker paging + sort" entry.) (**The brightness preview can be pointed at a variation with option dropdowns (working tree, product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** The `Viewer brightness` panel on the 3D views tab now renders one `<select>` per variation option above the preview; a full combination resolves to a `svr_variants` child and shows that child's model, a part-filled one (any option left on **Any**) falls back to the product's own. (**The stage viewer keeps the shopper's viewing angle and zoom when an option change swaps the model (working tree, product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** `Viewer3d.tsx` captures camera position/target, pivot turn and the touch latches into a module-scope `carriedView` at dispose and re-applies them on the next build - module-scope because the painted/unpainted stage boundary remounts the component; honoured only within a 3s freshness window so a client-side navigation elsewhere still opens at the default framing; applied after OrbitControls saves its state, so Reset view still means the opening framing - see the module's "Carried view" entry.) (**The material configurator can paint from a product ATTRIBUTE, not only a variation option (working tree, product-3d-views-for-shop, unreleased).** A slot's `colourOptionId` now also accepts a `pat_attributes` id, stored `attr:`-prefixed so the two id spaces cannot collide (`readColourSource` in `lib/fabric/constants.ts` is the shared reader; unprefixed still means an option, so saved configs need no migration).
