- `app/sitemap.ts` - site URL root plus all published InfoPage slugs.

Pages (status screens, reached only by proxy rewrite):

- `/cactus-status/coming-soon` - `statusPage` Layout (ctx `siteStatus: 'coming_soon'`) or fallback card. `force-dynamic`, noindex.
- `/cactus-status/maintenance` - same with `maintenance`; fallback "Down for maintenance" card.

Pages (setup):

- `/setup` - `app/setup/page.tsx` - client wizard, three steps: `connect` (Vercel token + project selection via `/api/setup/vercel-connect`), `database` (sub-states for Vercel bootstrap, Neon auto-provision, existing-project reuse, manual DATABASE_URL, local mode), `configure` (admin account + passkey or TOTP, admin path, site essentials, optional env vars, complete). Polls `/api/health` and `/api/setup/env-check` across the redeploys it triggers.
- `app/setup/layout.tsx` - `setup-shell` wrapper, noindex, absolute title.

Pages (member area, live under internal `/cactus-account/*`, reached only via the rewritten `/<memberAreaPath>/*` - Phases 1-3 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md):

- `/{memberAreaPath}/register` - `app/(public)/cactus-account/register/page.tsx` - server component: 404-styled message when `membersConfig.enabled` is false; in `INVITE_ONLY` mode, validates `?invite=` server-side and shows an "invite-only" message instead of the form when missing/invalid; otherwise renders `RegisterForm` with the resolved privacy-policy page link.
- `/{memberAreaPath}/verify-email` - `app/(public)/cactus-account/verify-email/page.tsx` - client page (wrapped in `Suspense` for `useSearchParams`); with a `?token=`, POSTs it to the verify API and shows the result; always offers an email field + "resend" button (60s client-side countdown mirroring the server throttle), enumeration-safe.
- `/{memberAreaPath}/login` - `app/(public)/cactus-account/login/page.tsx` - server component reading `redirect`/`magic_token` straight from `searchParams` (no client `useSearchParams`, so no Suspense boundary needed); sanitises `redirect` via the shared `sanitizeRedirect` in `lib/auth/redirect.ts` (an earlier inline copy omitted the `/\` backslash guard, so `/\evil.com` normalised to `//evil.com` post-login). Renders `LoginForm`.
- `components/members/RegisterForm.tsx` - client form: email/username/display name, privacy-policy consent checkbox, optional `TurnstileWidget`, submits to `POST /api/members/register`; redirects to `verify-email?email=…` when verification is required, else shows the final status inline (PENDING_APPROVAL vs ACTIVE copy).
- `components/members/LoginForm.tsx` - client form: email + "sign in with passkey" (falls back to a no-passkey message) or "email me a sign-in link"; auto-consumes a `?magic_token=` on mount; either path redirects to `verify-email` on a `redirectToVerify` rejection, else to the sanitised `redirectTo`.
- `components/members/TurnstileWidget.tsx` - loads the Cloudflare Turnstile script on demand and renders/tears down a widget instance; reads/writes `window.turnstile` via a local type cast rather than a global `Window` augmentation, because `modules/gazette`'s comment form already augments `Window.turnstile` with a narrower shape and TypeScript requires merged global augmentations to match exactly - core must not depend on or collide with an optional module's globals.
- `/{memberAreaPath}` + 5 sections (`app/(public)/cactus-account/{layout.tsx,page.tsx,profile,security,notifications,activity,danger-zone}`) - session-gated (redirects to `login?redirect=…` otherwise); `layout.tsx` also shows a cancellable deletion-grace banner and the `AccountNav.tsx` tab bar (reuses `components/admin/TabStrip.tsx`), filtered by `membersConfig.accountSectionsEnabled`. Overview (`page.tsx`) also renders any `members.account-section` extension-point contributions (content-injection only, not a new nav tab). `ProfileSection.tsx` (avatar, displayName/bio/website, per-field visibility toggles), `SecuritySection.tsx` (passkeys, password, 2FA incl. QR setup, sessions, trusted browsers, recovery codes - the single biggest client component), `NotificationsSection.tsx`, `ActivitySection.tsx`, `DangerZoneSection.tsx` (data export request/download/expiry via a blob-download helper - same pattern as `app/cactus-admin/account/page.tsx`'s `handleExport`, not a raw `<a href>`, deletion request/cancel).

Pages (public member profile, Phase 4 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md - fixed paths, no proxy rewrite involved):

- `/members/[username]` - `app/(public)/members/[username]/page.tsx` - see the Middleware/Authentication sections for the full visibility matrix; old-username redirect; `members.profile-section` extension point.
- `/members` - `app/(public)/members/page.tsx` - paginated directory (24/page), gated on `directoryEnabled`.
- `components/members/MemberAvatar.tsx`, `GeneratedAvatar.tsx` - see Media Layer section.

Pages (admin, live under internal `/cactus-admin/*`, reached only via the rewritten `/<adminPath>/*`):

- `/cactus-admin` - dashboard: page/user/media counts, site-status badge, optional-feature checklist (media, email, Turnstile, Edge Config, GitHub, Sentry) with links into Settings tabs. Below that, a generic grid renders any module's contributions to the `core.admin-dashboard-widgets` extension point (permission-filtered live from `Module.manifest.extensionPoints`, same pattern as the Settings → Users → Roles subtab's `core.roles-page` section) - currently Boards' `boardsDashboardWidget` (thread/post/open-queue counts, link into the module admin).
- `/cactus-admin/login` - server `page.tsx` wrapper (calls `resolveBranding()`, passes `siteName`/`faviconUrl`/`faviconDarkUrl` down) + `LoginForm.tsx` ('use client', the whole former page): passkey (default, WebAuthn prompt fires automatically on page load unless a recovery token is in the URL; fallback options hidden behind "Use another way to sign in" until the auto attempt fails/is cancelled - a cancelled auto attempt (`NotAllowedError`) shows no error banner), password → email OTP (trust-device checkbox), authenticator (TOTP), recovery-token completion, no-passkey fallbacks (register new passkey or recovery email), lost-access instructions including Neon console link. Logo above "Sign in" shows the site's uploaded favicon (light/dark variant swap via `data-logo-variant`, same mechanism as the admin sidebar logo) falling back to the Cactus mark when the admin hasn't set one.
- `/cactus-admin/account` - profile (displayName), change email, passkeys add/remove, TOTP set-up/remove, password add/change (with sign-out-other-sessions), active sessions list/revoke, GDPR JSON export, self-delete account. Split into a server `page.tsx` wrapper + `AccountPageClient.tsx` ('use client', the whole former page): the wrapper resolves `admins.account-section` extension-point contributions (permission-filtered live from `Module.manifest`, same pattern as the dashboard's `core.admin-dashboard-widgets`) and passes them via an `extensionSections` prop, rendered between the "Your data" row and the Delete account card. First consumer: Twilio's `TwilioAdminSmsSection` (self-service SMS login-code enrolment).
- `/cactus-admin/pages` - InfoPage list with pagination, bulk select + delete (`PagesTable.tsx`); gated per `pages.write`/`pages.delete`.
- `/cactus-admin/pages/new` - title/slug form (+ optional menu assignment when `menus.manage`), creates a builder-format draft then opens the editor.
- `/cactus-admin/pages/[id]` - full-screen Puck editor (`PuckEditor.tsx`): content only saves on an explicit Update/Publish click (no background autosave - **changed 2026-07-08**, was 1.5s debounced), gated on `pages.publish`, preview link, delete. Unsaved edits trigger a `beforeunload` warning and a confirm on the in-app back link. Sidebar gained Settings/SEO/History/Saved Blocks tabs (see Puck Integration) - History tab lists live + up to 10 archived versions with restore into editor. Markdown pages are silently migrated to builder format on open.
- `/cactus-admin/menus` - menu list: create, rename, delete (with main-menu warning), item counts, a Created column + "empty" badge, a name filter (shown when >1 menu), **Set as main** (promote to header menu without leaving the page), and **Duplicate** (deep-clone the whole menu + items). Create/rename inputs take Escape-to-cancel; create is blocked client-side on a duplicate (case-insensitive) name.
- `/cactus-admin/menus/[id]` - menu item editor: add page/module-content/external items, edit label/url/new-tab, delete. Reordering: drag a row via its handle, or use ↑/↓ (siblings-only swap, keyboard/click-friendly, no native drag required). Per-row actions are Edit/Delete plus a "⋯" kebab: a **Who can see this** section (Everyone / Signed-in only / Signed-out only / Admins only → `PATCH item {visibility}`), add child item (pre-sets the parent; disabled past the 3-level depth cap), promote one level if nested, and a depth-aware "nest under" select. Non-PUBLIC items show an inline audience badge (Members/Guests/Admins only). A header summary line counts items · limited-visibility · needs-attention; **attention badges** flag a deleted page/entity (error) or a draft page / unpublished entity that's hidden from the live site (warning). Destination cell links out (PAGE → page editor, external/module → live URL, new tab). An item filter (matches label/destination, keeps whole matching branches; disables drag/reorder while active) and Collapse all / Expand all (per-parent chevrons) tame large menus. Add-item lightbox has a "Who can see this?" picker and Escape-to-close. Header shows a "Main menu" badge when this menu is the one assigned in Settings → General.
- `/cactus-admin/media` - media library with folders + tags (redesigned 2026-07-13: full restructure). Server `page.tsx` loads the flat folder list (+ per-folder + root media counts), the tag list (+ counts), the root's first page (`queryMediaLibrary`), AND a whole-library overview (`computeLibraryStats`, `lib/media/library-stats.ts` - one pass over every row + the usage index: `totalFiles/totalSize/imageFiles/optimisedFiles/optimisableFiles/unusedFiles/unusedSize`), then hands off to `MediaLibrary.tsx` (client orchestrator). Layout top-to-bottom: page header (title + `MediaUpload`); `MediaStatsBar.tsx` (4 tiles - Files[+folder count], Storage used, Unused→click filters to unused, Optimisable→click filters to images; the two action tiles take a warning/info accent while there's work and drill into the WHOLE library via a `browseAll` flag); then a `minmax(180-220px,1fr)` split of `FolderTree.tsx` sidebar + content. `FolderTree` is unchanged behaviourally (recursive/expandable, path-to-current force-open, each row a nav button + `(count)` + drop target, folder rows draggable to move via `PATCH /api/admin/media/folders/[id]` `{parentId}` [self/descendant drops rejected by `isDescendant`], rows accept OS files dropped onto them when `media.upload`, hover rename/delete icons, "+ New folder") plus a new `browsingAll` prop that drops the active-row highlight while a search/tag/stat drill-down spans all folders. Content: breadcrumb (Media / … drop targets; shows "All folders" when spanning the tree), `MediaToolbar.tsx` (search-all box, sort/type/usage/tag selects, a grid|list **view toggle** persisted to `localStorage['cactus.media.view']`, and a removable **active-filter chip** strip + "Clear all"), a sticky selection/clipboard bar (Cut/Copy/Move to…/Optimise/Change ratio…/Resize…/Delete/Paste-here/Clear), then either a **grid** of `MediaCard.tsx` or a dense **list** `MediaList.tsx` (table: select-all header, thumb, sortable Name/Size/Uploaded headers wired to the sort state, Type, Folder, Usage pill; rows draggable + right-click + row-click-to-open). Nav/sort/filter/search/tag changes refetch `GET /api/admin/media` (first render reuses server items via a `firstRun` ref; `folderScope='all'` when search/tag/`browseAll`); further pages via an `IntersectionObserver` sentinel. Content pane + folder rows are OS-file drop targets (when `media.upload`) → `POST /api/admin/media`. Cards/rows are draggable (dragging a selected one drags the whole selection) onto any tree node/breadcrumb → `POST /api/admin/media/move`. Right-click opens `ContextMenu` (Open details / Optimise[raster unoptimised] / Replace file…[library-accepted types] / Edit image…[raster] / Change ratio…[raster] / Resize…[raster] / Cut / Copy / Paste here / Rename… / Move to… / Tags…[opens the detail panel] / Delete); Cut/Copy fill a clipboard (cut items dimmed), Paste calls `/move` (cut) or `/duplicate` (copy). Opening a thumbnail/row opens **`MediaDetailPanel.tsx`** - a right-hand **slide-over** that replaced the old full-screen `MediaLightbox`: large preview, In use/Optimised badges, metadata (type/size/folder/alt/uploaded), an **inline tag editor** (type-to-create + autocomplete, Save/Reset, `PUT /api/admin/media/[id]/tags`), Prev/Next with ArrowLeft/Right (ignored while typing), and an action footer (Open original / Optimise[raster unopt, `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/optimise`] / Replace file…[library-accepted types] / Edit image… / Change ratio… / Resize… / Rename… / Move… / Cut / Copy / Delete). Rename (`NameDialog`) / move (`MoveDialog`) / folder rename+delete (`NameDialog`/`DeleteFolderDialog`) / name-clash (`CollisionDialog` Keep both=suffix/Replace/Skip[move]/Cancel) dialogs are unchanged. Delete (single or bulk) always runs the in-use warning flow (`POST /bulk-delete` without force → still-referenced items return in `skipped`, dialog switches to "Delete anyway"). Edit image… opens `MediaImageEditor.tsx` (unchanged: crop box w/ 8 handles + rule-of-thirds + aspect presets Free/1:1/3:2/4:3/16:9/2:3/3:4/9:16 + custom W:H, "Save (replaces original)" [confirm] / "Save as new…" [filename], posts the source-pixel crop rect to `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/edit`). **Change ratio…** opens `MediaAspectDialog.tsx` (new 2026-07-16) - reshapes one image (detail panel / context menu) or the whole selection (selection bar) to a target ratio by **padding**, never cropping or stretching: ratio presets 1:1/3:2/4:3/16:9/2:3/3:4/9:16 + custom W:H, fill picker (Blurred image [default] / Colour [`<input type=color>` + White/Black shortcuts] / Transparent), a live CSS preview mirroring the server output (contain + pad; chequerboard for transparent), and Save-as-new [default] vs Replace-original [confirm step]. Transparent is disabled and derived away when any selected item is a JPEG (mirrors `supportsTransparentFill`). Bulk 'new' sends no `newName` (one name across many would collide) so the server suffixes each with the ratio. Posts to `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/aspect` (single) or `POST /api/admin/media/bulk-aspect` (bulk). **Resize…** opens `MediaResizeDialog.tsx` (new 2026-07-17) - aimed the same three ways (detail panel / context menu / selection bar), scales one image or the whole selection **down** to fit a box, keeping the ratio and never enlarging: longest-edge presets Extra large 2400 / Large 1600 / Medium 1000 / Small 600 (each sent as `{width: px, height: px}` so fit-inside caps the longest edge whichever way round the image is) + custom W/H (either side blank = unconstrained), a preview, and Save-as-new [default] vs Replace-original [confirm step]. `Media` has **no width/height columns**, so the dialog reads `naturalWidth`/`naturalHeight` off the loaded preview `<img>` purely to show "is 4000x3000, would become 1600x1200" and to disable the button when a single image already fits - the server measures the real bytes itself and is the authority. Bulk sends no `newName` (collision) so the server suffixes each with its own new size; the bulk toast reports `bytesSaved`. Posts to `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/resize` (single) or `POST /api/admin/media/bulk-resize` (bulk). `isReshapable` renamed `isRasterImage` in `MediaLibrary.tsx` (+ `reshapableSelected` → `rasterSelected`) - reshape and resize want the same predicate for the same reason. **All mutations report via toast notifications** (`MediaToasts.tsx`, bottom-right stack) instead of the old layout-shifting inline error/busy lines; a persistent "busy" toast shows while an op runs. Shared helpers: `format.ts` (bytes/date/filename/kind), `types.ts` (`LibraryItem`/`TagInfo`/`Sort`/`TypeFilter`/`UseFilter`/`ViewMode`/`SORTS`). In-use status computed via `lib/media/references.ts`. `MediaCard.tsx` slimmed (thumbnail, filename, kind·size, usage dot, ✓ Optimised badge, tag chips, hover-revealed select checkbox - no more per-card Optimise/Delete buttons). REMOVED: `MediaLightbox.tsx`, `MediaDelete.tsx` (single-delete UI folded into the bulk-delete in-use flow); `MediaGrid.tsx` was already gone. Below the library, `page.tsx` renders **`MediaStorageCheck.tsx`** (new 2026-07-19) when the viewer holds `config.manage` - an on-demand "Storage check" card (never part of the server render: it lists every object the providers hold) with a Run check button, then three groups (Leftover files / Files that have gone / Sizes recorded wrongly), each capped at 20 listed rows with an "…and N more". "Correct these" posts `correct-sizes`; "Delete all leftovers" (only when `media.delete`) confirms then posts `delete-orphans`; both re-scan afterwards rather than patching the list client-side.
- `/cactus-admin/appearance` - server redirect to `/appearance/styles`.
- `/cactus-admin/appearance/styles` - design-token editor (v2 tokens): tabs colours/typography/headings/buttons/images/formFields/spacing, colour presets, ~50 Google-font list, saves via `PATCH /api/admin/appearance`. Every colour field (global palette + all `themeStyle` colours: background, links, body, caption, display, h1-h6, buttons + hover, image border, form fields) offers an optional **dark-mode override**; `ColourInput` renders a light row plus a "Dark mode override (optional)" sub-row via the shared `ColourPickerRow` helper (native colour picker + palette swatches using each global colour's dark variant). Overrides persist as parallel `*Dark` keys on the design tokens; unset = reuse the light colour. Colour presets also seed dark-mode link colours (`ColourPreset.linkColourDark`/`linkHoverColourDark`), so applying one sets both light and dark links. Headings tab: a site-wide **Headings font (all headings)** `FontPickerField` at the top of the Headings section, stored as `themeStyle.headingsFont` (optional string; per-level `family` overrides it, empty inherits the body font) - `buildTokenStyles` merges it as the family fallback into every `h1`-`h6` (vars + `main hN` scoped rules) and Display, and `buildFontHref` loads it (incl. per-level weights on inheriting levels); the "Display (hero heading, largest - above H1)" section was REMOVED from the tab (its `setDisplay` helper too) - `themeStyle.display` tokens/emission stay honoured for existing rows and the Heading block's display level, there's just no UI editing them any more. Colours tab also has a **Status boxes** section: one accent colour per Callout type (info/success/warning/error, `STATUS_KEYS`) with optional dark override, stored as `themeStyle.status`; `buildTokenStyles` derives `--status-{key}` (accent), `--status-{key}-bg` (tint towards white in light / black in dark) and `--status-{key}-title` per mode via `statusVars()`. The Buttons and Form Fields tabs each end with a **sticky bottom live preview** (`StickyPreview` + `ButtonsPreview`/`FormFieldsPreview` in `page.tsx`): light and dark panes on the site's page-background colours, styles computed inline from the current unsaved token state (fallbacks mirror the ButtonLink block and contact-form field defaults), with the tokens' Google fonts loaded in-admin via a `buildFontHref` `<link>`. Buttons tab also has **Secondary variant**/**Outline variant** sections (`buttons.secondary`/`.outline`, each optional colour set + hover, `setButtonVariant`/`setButtonVariantHover` helpers) styling the ButtonLink block's other two options independently of Primary; `ButtonsPreview` renders all three. Colours tab has a **Badges** section (`themeStyle.badges`, `BADGE_COLOUR_KEYS` = blue/yellow/red/gray, each `{bg,text,+Dark}`, `setBadge` helper) plus a **Badge / pill corner radius** field (`themeStyle.pillRadius`, `setPillRadius`) shared by the Badge and Eyebrow blocks.
- `/cactus-admin/layouts` - layout cards filtered by type tab (all/header/footer/infoPage/notFound/statusPage + one per module group), each with a `LayoutPreview` thumbnail, display-condition summary, and Edit/Preview/Duplicate/Delete. Every layout is editable and deletable (no starter rows, no read-only cards). "+ New Layout" carries the active tab's type through as `?type=`. Name/description **search box** with an `n of m` count in the `TabStrip` trailing slot; tab switches are guarded by a request token so a slow earlier fetch cannot land under a later tab. Status badge reads the conditions, not just the column: **Live** (published with ≥1 complete include rule), **Not shown** (published but no rule that matches anything - it renders nowhere), **Draft**. Delete uses an in-app dialog that says out loud when the layout it is about to remove is live on the site (the old `window.confirm` could not).
- `/cactus-admin/layouts/new` - the starter picker. One tabbed page (shared `TabStrip` + `lib/layout/layout-type-tabs.ts`, second-level tabs for a module group's sub-types), a card per starter template with a `LayoutPreview` drawing of its structure. Clicking a card `POST`s the template's `data` to `/api/admin/layouts` and routes straight into the builder - no naming step, the layout takes the template's name and is renamed in the editor's Settings tab. Templates come from `getStarterTemplates(type)` (in-code, imported directly - no fetch). Replaces the old 3-step wizard (type → sub-type → name + starter radio list). **Module group tabs (and so their templates) appear only if the site has that module installed** - see the module-layout-types entry under Puck Integration.
- `/cactus-admin/layouts/[id]` - layout Puck editor (`LayoutPuckEditor.tsx`, 1.2s debounced autosave). Sidebar gained Settings/Conditions/History/Saved Blocks tabs (see Puck Integration) - Conditions tab is `DisplayConditionsPanel` (include/exclude rules; publish requires ≥1 **complete** include rule - Save is disabled while any rule still has a blank value, and `module` rules finally get a text input, having previously been unfillable), History tab lists live + up to 10 archived versions with restore into editor (restore asks before it fetches, and a published layout's restore re-publishes so the replaced version is archived rather than lost).
- `/cactus-admin/users` - unified People table (`PeopleListClient.tsx`, self-fetching `GET /api/admin/people`): staff (User) and site members (Member) in one search+paginate list, a type badge distinguishing them, and a Role-or-status column; staff rows keep the role select / suspend / delete actions (`UserActions.tsx`, non-admins cannot act on protected-role users), member rows link out to `/cactus-admin/members/[id]` for the full suspend/trust/approve/delete action set (bulk multi-select on members was dropped in the merge - use the per-member page, or the still-present but now UI-unlinked `GET/POST /api/admin/members/bulk`).
- `/cactus-admin/modules` - module directory (org `cactus-foundation-modules`), install with public/beta channel choice, update / enable / disable / uninstall (code-only or code+data teardown), per-module update channel, release-notes modal, stale-`deploying` reconciliation, "Update all" button (shown when ≥1 module has an update pending) batching all pending module updates into a single deploy.
- `/cactus-admin/notifications` - notification list with per-type icon, reasons list, read/unread toggle, delete, "Redeploy now" for open deployment notifications (`NotificationActions.tsx`).
- `/cactus-admin/config` - Settings, 8 core tabs + module-registered tabs (see Admin UI section). Server component fetches active modules' `manifest.settingsTabs`, permission-filters, passes to client `ConfigPageClient`.
- `/cactus-admin/config/privacy-generator` - 6-step privacy-policy wizard; assembles markdown from `lib/privacy/template.ts` and creates a draft InfoPage, optionally linking it as the privacy policy page.
- `/cactus-admin/m/[module]/[...path]` - generic module page host; delegates to `resolveModulePage` in generated `lib/modules/router.ts`.
- `app/cactus-admin/layout.tsx` - admin shell: reads `x-cactus-admin-path` / `x-cactus-is-login` headers, secondary session check, module nav entries from `Module.manifest.navEntries` (permission-filtered), unread notification count, admin white-labelling (primary colour family + sans font only). Nav entries are grouped: a module with no `manifest.navGroupLabel` renders as plain links directly under Dashboard, no section heading (currently just contact-form's Inbox); a module that sets `navGroupLabel` (Gazette `"Gazette"`, Boards `"Boards"`) gets its own `admin-nav-section-label` heading with just its own links, rendered after the System section - both via `AdminShell`/`AdminNav`'s `moduleNavGroups` prop (`Array<{label: string|null, links}>`), split in `AdminNav.tsx` into `ungroupedModuleLinks` (flattened, no header) vs `labelledModuleGroups` (own collapsible section).

API route handlers (core):

- `GET /api/health` - `SELECT 1` liveness check; `{status, database: connected|disconnected}`.
- `GET/POST /api/consent` - GDPR consent record append (action, decision map validated against configured categories, truncated IP, SHA-256 UA hash; sets 2-year `cactus-consent-id` httpOnly cookie); GET returns the latest decision for the cookie's consentId.
- `POST /api/webhooks/vercel` - HMAC-SHA1 signature check against `VERCEL_WEBHOOK_SECRET`; on `deployment.succeeded` for the tracked deployment: promotes `deploying` modules, releases DeployLock, clears the redeploy gate; on error/canceled: rolls modules back and resolves the `'pending'` sentinel to the real deployment id.
- `GET|POST|PATCH|DELETE /api/m/[module]/[...path]` - generic module API dispatcher via generated `lib/modules/router.ts`; `force-dynamic`, `maxDuration = 60`.

Auth API:

- `GET /api/auth/config` - public: `emailConfigured`, `turnstileConfigured`, `turnstileSiteKey`. **`neonProjectId` was removed (2026-07-23)** - this payload is served before anyone authenticates, and the project id is infrastructure metadata that nothing on the login screen actually needs; `LoginForm.tsx` no longer reads it and its lost-passkey help now links to the plain `https://console.neon.tech` rather than a project deep link.
- `POST /api/auth/login` - password step of password+OTP login; 503 when email unconfigured; Turnstile; rate limit (`login`, ip+account_email); constant-time-ish hash compare; sends 6-digit `login_otp` EmailChallenge; returns `{step:'otp', userId}`.
- `POST /api/auth/email-code` - verifies the OTP (skipped when trusted-device cookie valid); creates session; optional trusted-device cookie for `trustDeviceDays`. Rejects a suspended account (`suspendedAt`) before minting the session, matching the password/TOTP/passkey mint sites.
- `POST /api/auth/logout` - deletes session, clears cookie, redirects `/logged-out`.
- `POST /api/auth/passkey/authenticate-options` - rate limited; if the given email's account has zero passkeys returns `{noPasskeys: true}` and **no userId** (handing an internal id to an unauthenticated caller was step 1 of an account takeover); else WebAuthn authentication options (challenge stored in `WebAuthnChallenge`, 5 min TTL). User verification is `required`.
- `POST /api/auth/passkey/authenticate-verify` - verifies assertion (challenge extracted from `clientDataJSON`), suspended check, creates session, updates passkey counter. `requireUserVerification: true`.
- `POST /api/auth/passkey/register-options` - Origin must match SITE_URL (rpId guard); a body `userId` is honoured **only while the setup bootstrap window is open** (`isSetupBootstrapOpen`, `lib/auth/setup-window.ts`), otherwise the target is taken from the session and the body value ignored; excludeCredentials from existing passkeys; stable WebAuthn user handle encoded from userId.
- `POST /api/auth/passkey/register-verify` - session required outside the setup window; target userId comes from the stored challenge (not spoofable from the body) and must equal the signed-in user, else 403; labels the passkey from the user agent.
- `POST /api/auth/passkey/register-login` - **DELETED** (security). It registered a passkey and minted a session for any account with zero passkeys, using nothing but a body `userId` as the identity claim - a full takeover of any staff account that had never enrolled one. A passkey is now only ever added to an already-authenticated session (or during first-run setup); the login page offers password / authenticator / recovery link instead.
- `POST /api/auth/totp/setup-options` - generates a TOTP secret (base32, 20 bytes), otpauth URI and QR data URL; secret stored encrypted (AES-256-GCM via `ENCRYPTION_KEY`), unverified; body userId trusted only pre-setup.
- `POST /api/auth/totp/setup-verify` - verifies the first code (window ±1, replay-guarded via `totpLastStep`), sets `totpVerifiedAt`; setup-wizard mode also creates the session.
- `POST /api/auth/totp/verify` - email+code login; single generic error to prevent account enumeration; rate limited; creates session.
- `POST /api/auth/recovery/request` - always returns 200 (no enumeration); Turnstile; rate limited; emails a recovery link (`/api/auth/recovery/complete?token=…`, 30 min TTL) plus a "recovery requested" notification.
- `GET /api/auth/recovery/complete` - validates the token then redirects to `/<adminPath>/login?recovery_token=…`.
- `POST /api/auth/recovery/complete` - validates the optional new password FIRST and only then consumes the token (a rejected password no longer burns the link), invalidates all sessions and trusted devices, creates a fresh session, sends a completion notification email.

Members API (Phase 1 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md - registration/verification only; no member session system yet, so nothing here requires or issues a member auth cookie):

- `POST /api/members/register` - 403 when `membersConfig.enabled` is false; Turnstile; rate limit `member_register` (5/60min per IP, `lib/auth/rate-limit.ts`); `INVITE_ONLY` mode requires and validates+consumes a `MemberInvite` token; email domain allow/blocklist (`isEmailDomainAllowed`); username format/blocklist/uniqueness; email uniqueness (409); creates the `Member` row (status `PENDING_VERIFICATION` when verification is required and email is configured, else immediately `ACTIVE`/`PENDING_APPROVAL` per `registrationMode` - see `deriveInitialStatus`/`deriveActivatedStatus` in `lib/members/registration.ts`); writes a `MemberConsentRecord` (`privacy_policy`); sends a plain (non-templated - Phase 6 adds `EmailTemplate`) verification email via `sendVerificationEmail`.
- `POST /api/members/verify-email` - consumes a `MemberVerificationToken` (24h TTL, single-use, `lib/members/tokens.ts`); on success moves the member from `PENDING_VERIFICATION` to `PENDING_APPROVAL` or `ACTIVE` per `registrationMode`.
- `POST /api/members/verify-email/resend` - enumeration-safe: always `{ok:true}` regardless of whether the email exists, is already verified, or is throttled; resends only when the member is `PENDING_VERIFICATION` and the 60-second per-member throttle (`canResendVerification`) has elapsed.
- `POST /api/members/auth/passkey/authenticate-options` - rate limited (shared `passkey_authenticate` bucket with admin); given an email resolving to an ACTIVE member with zero passkeys, returns `{noPasskeys: true}` (deliberately no memberId - members have no bootstrap flow to feed it into, see `lib/members/passkey.ts` note); any other case (not found, or found but not ACTIVE) falls through to a generic unscoped challenge so the shape never reveals account existence/status.
- `POST /api/members/auth/passkey/authenticate-verify` - verifies the assertion, rejects via `loginRejectionForStatus` for any non-ACTIVE member, else creates a `MemberSession` + sets the `cactus_member_session` cookie.
- `POST /api/members/auth/passkey/register-options`, `POST /api/members/auth/passkey/register-verify` - add a passkey to the *signed-in* member (`getMemberFromCookie`, 401 without a session); register-verify cross-checks the challenge's stored `memberId` against the session's member before saving.
- `POST /api/members/auth/magic-link/request` - enumeration-safe (always `{ok:true}`); rate limited (`member_magic_link`, 5/15min/IP); sends whenever the member exists, regardless of status (status is gated at consume time, not here); no-ops when magic-link isn't enabled/allowed.
- `POST /api/members/auth/magic-link/consume` - single-use, 15-min TTL; `loginRejectionForStatus` gate; creates the `MemberSession` + cookie on success.
- `POST /api/members/auth/password/login` - password step (requires `passwordsEnabled`); skips 2FA when the browser is trusted; else `{step:'2fa', method}`; 403 if 2FA is mandatory but not yet configured for that member. Trusted-browser `done` responses also carry `smsEnrolmentRequired` (see `lib/members/sms-policy.ts`) so the login form can land the member on the account overview's enrolment card.
- `POST /api/members/auth/2fa/verify` - second factor (EMAIL code or TOTP, whichever the member has), optional `trustBrowser`; creates the session; success response carries `smsEnrolmentRequired` (same contract as the login route).
- `POST /api/members/auth/recovery-code/consume` - one-time code as a 2FA fallback; creates the session.
- `POST /api/members/auth/logout` - clears the session + cookie, redirects `/logged-out`.
- `POST /api/members/auth/logout-all` - session-gated; deletes every `MemberSession` for the member (including the caller's own - forces full re-auth).
- `GET /api/members/auth/config` - public: `allowedAuthMethods`, `passwordsEnabled`, `turnstileSiteKey`.

Member account API (Phase 3 of MEMBERS_SPEC.md; every route below requires a member session via `getMemberFromCookie`, 401 otherwise):

- `GET/PATCH /api/members/profile` - displayName/bio/websiteUrl. Username is read-only here (change-with-cooldown is Phase 4).
- `POST/DELETE /api/members/avatar` - upload (gated on `avatarUploadsEnabled` + media provider configured; replaces and deletes any previous uploaded avatar) / remove (falls back to GRAVATAR or GENERATED per `gravatarEnabled`).
- `GET/DELETE /api/members/sessions`, `DELETE /api/members/sessions/[id]` - list (current flagged via `isCurrent`) / revoke-all-but-current / revoke one.
- `GET /api/members/passkeys`, `DELETE /api/members/passkeys/[id]` - list / remove, with a lockout guard: refuses to delete the last passkey unless `MAGIC_LINK` is an allowed auth method or a password exists (members always have magic link as a fallback if it's enabled, unlike admin whose only fallback is a password).
- `GET/POST/DELETE /api/members/password` - status (`hasPassword`, `hasTwoFactor`, `passwordsEnabled`) / add-or-change (`signOutOtherSessions` option) / remove.
- `GET/DELETE /api/members/2fa` - status / remove (refused with a clear error while a password still exists, since 2FA is mandatory whenever one is set).
- `POST /api/members/2fa/setup-options` - EMAIL sends a code; AUTHENTICATOR_APP returns a QR + secret (stored unverified).
- `POST /api/members/2fa/setup-verify` - verifies either method; a member has one active method at a time (setting a new one deletes the other); auto-generates and returns recovery codes once, only on the member's *first* successful 2FA setup ever.
- `GET/DELETE /api/members/trusted-browsers`, `DELETE .../[id]` - list (current flagged) / revoke-all / revoke one.
- `GET/POST /api/members/recovery-codes` - remaining count / regenerate (requires 2FA already configured; shown once).
- `GET/PATCH /api/members/notifications` - categories are entirely module-contributed (`getModuleNotificationCategories`) - core has none of its own yet.
- `GET /api/members/activity` - last 50 `MemberActivityEvent` rows.
- `GET/POST /api/members/data-export`, `GET /api/members/data-export/download` - GET returns the latest request's status; POST runs the whole assemble→upload→ready flow synchronously within the request (`maxDuration = 60`, same "no background job system" constraint the Gazette/Boards importers already accept) and refuses a second request while one is `PENDING`/`PROCESSING`; download streams the stored JSON back through this authenticated route rather than ever handing the browser the underlying (if unguessable) storage URL, since this file contains personal data unlike ordinary public media.
- `POST /api/members/delete-account`, `POST /api/members/cancel-deletion` - sets/clears `deletionRequestedAt`/`deletionScheduledAt` (grace period from `membersConfig.deletionGracePeriodDays`).
- `GET/PATCH /api/members/profile-visibility` - per-field public-profile show/hide (`showBio`/`showJoinDate`/`showWebsite`).
- `POST /api/members/username` - Phase 4; requires `usernameChangesEnabled`; `usernameChangeCooldownDays` off `usernameChangedAt`; stamps `previousUsername`/`previousUsernameExpiresAt` (`usernameRedirectDays`) so `/members/[username]` can redirect old links.
- `GET /api/members/avatar-proxy/[id]` - public, no session required; Phase 4 - see Media Layer section.

Member cron routes (`Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET`, same pattern as module crons):

- `GET /api/cron/members/purge` - hard-deletes every member whose `deletionScheduledAt` has passed (cascades take every child row per the schema).
- `GET /api/cron/members/exports` - expires every `READY` data-export request past its 48h `expiresAt`, deleting the underlying media file.
- `GET /api/cron/members/digest?mode=daily|weekly` - see the Email section for what a digest actually batches.

Account API (all require session):

- `DELETE /api/account` - self-deletion in a transaction; blocked when it would leave zero active admins; InfoPage/Media/ConsentRecord ownership nulled.
- `GET/PATCH /api/account/profile` - email/username/displayName; PATCH displayName (max 128).
- `POST /api/account/email` - change email; requires current password when one is set; 409 on conflict.
- `GET/POST /api/account/password` - status (`hasPassword`, `emailConfigured`); add/change password (refused when email unconfigured; breached-password check; optional sign-out-other-sessions preserving the current one by token hash).
- `GET /api/account/passkeys`, `DELETE /api/account/passkeys/[id]` - list; deletion of the last passkey blocked unless a password exists.
- `GET/DELETE /api/account/sessions`, `DELETE /api/account/sessions/[id]` - list (current session flagged), revoke all, revoke one.
- `GET/DELETE /api/account/totp` - enabled status; removal blocked when TOTP is the only sign-in method.
- `GET /api/account/export` - GDPR Art. 20 JSON download: profile, role, passkey metadata (no key material), active sessions, consent records.

Admin API:

- `GET/PATCH /api/admin/config` - `config.manage`. GET returns the full SiteConfig row plus derived branding preview URLs `logoUrl`/`logoDarkUrl`/`faviconUrl`/`faviconDarkUrl`/`appIconUrl`/`appleTouchUrl`/`icon192Url`/`icon512Url` (media rows resolved via a shared `lookup` helper for the Branding tab). PATCH validates every field with zod (incl. all branding media ids `logoMediaId`/`logoDarkMediaId`/`faviconMediaId`/`faviconDarkMediaId`/`appIconMediaId`/`appleTouchIconMediaId`/`webManifest192MediaId`/`webManifest512MediaId` nullable, plus `appName`/`appShortName`/`themeColor`/`backgroundColor` text); adminPath blocklist; consent-banner "necessary" category enforced, `categoriesVersion`/`copyVersion` auto-bumped on meaningful changes; Edge Config sync for adminPath/status; a mediaProvider change returns a per-provider Media breakdown.
- `GET/PATCH /api/admin/appearance` - GET requires a valid session (public layout reads design tokens directly via Prisma, not this endpoint - only admin editors call it); PATCH requires `appearance.manage` and accepts only null or a `version: 2` token object.
- `GET/POST /api/admin/appearance/presets` and `PATCH/DELETE /api/admin/appearance/presets/[id]` - user-created colour presets (`UserColourPreset` model). GET requires a session; POST/PATCH/DELETE require `appearance.manage`. POST rejects a name that case-insensitively clashes with another user preset or a default `COLOUR_PRESETS` name (409). The Styles > Colours preset bar renders these rows first, then the hardcoded defaults; each user preset card gets a delete (✕) affordance the defaults don't have. The Save/Update button above the bar reads "Update preset" (PATCH, confirm-gated) when the current colours exactly match an existing user preset, else "Save as preset" (POST, opens a name-entry modal) - it never offers to overwrite a default preset.
- `GET/POST/DELETE /api/admin/env` - protected-role only; `maxDuration 60`. GET: boolean set/unset per allowlisted key (Vercel API, or `process.env` read-only in local mode). POST: upserts allowlisted vars to Vercel env, records a deployment-needed notification. The allowlist is `ALLOWED_KEYS` plus every installed module's manifest `requiredEnvVars` names (`getManagedKeys()`), minus the strictly protected infra keys (`PROTECTED_KEYS`: DATABASE_URL, SESSION_SECRET, SITE_URL, VERCEL_API_TOKEN, VERCEL_PROJECT_ID) - so module settings tabs (e.g. Twilio) can manage their own credentials without a core edit. DELETE ("Reset Everything"): deletes every project env var, writes the `pendingRedeployId: 'pending'` sentinel, triggers a redeploy in `after()`.
- `GET/PUT /api/admin/navigation` - `config.manage`. GET returns the stored `SiteConfig.adminMenuConfig` blob; PUT full-replaces it (zod `AdminMenuConfigSchema` from `lib/nav/admin-menu.ts`) - the admin-sidebar customisation (per-item order/rename/visibility) written by the Settings → Navigation builder. An empty `{items:{},sections:{}}` = back to built-in defaults.
- `POST /api/admin/config/test-email` - `config.manage`. Sends a test email to `to` (defaults to the caller's own email). Optional `credentials` body (`provider: 'brevo'|'smtp'` + key/host/port/user/pass strings) tests unsaved values typed into the settings form via `sendTestEmailWithCredentials` before a save/redeploy; blank fields fall back to the current server env. Without `credentials`, sends via the ordinary saved-env `sendTestEmail`.
- `POST /api/admin/branding/generate-icons` - `media.upload`. Body `{sourceMediaId}`; sharp resizes the uploaded app-icon source into favicon 96 / apple-touch 180 / PWA 192 / 512, stores each via `uploadMedia`+`saveMediaRecord`, returns ids+urls. Backs the Branding tab's one-shot App icon flow (see Admin UI).
- `POST /api/admin/media/deploy-worker` - protected-role, `maxDuration 60`. Uploads the Cloudflare media Worker to the user's account (creds from the request body, then the Vercel project's saved values, then `process.env`) and persists the CF creds + `CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL` via Vercel env. Every request field is optional once a deploy has succeeded. Backs the Media tab's "Set up the Worker automatically" box (see Admin UI / Media Layer).
- `GET /api/admin/github-app` - `config.manage` OR `modules.manage`; ENCRYPTION_KEY presence/format, GitHub App connection + installation state, `hasPat`.
- `GET/DELETE /api/admin/redeploy-status` - GET requires only a session (deliberately no permission gate; the admin shell's deploy status surfaces poll it for every admin role). DELETE (`config.manage`) clears the gate, releases DeployLock, reconciles `deploying` modules against the actual latest Vercel deployment state.
- `POST /api/admin/reset-database` - protected-role only. `deleteSetupData: true` = TRUNCATE all tables (preserving only adminPath) → setup wizard; the hard-reset TRUNCATE list now also includes `GithubAppConnection` (its encrypted App private key / webhook / client secrets have no FK into the old set and were surviving a factory reset), plus `SavedBlock`, `Folder`, `Tag`, `Notification`, `EmailTemplate`. Soft mode = truncate content tables, keep the current admin and SiteConfig, delete all other users, re-seed starter content (Home page, Main Menu, starter layouts, Styles page).
- `GET /api/admin/backup/database` - protected-role only, `maxDuration 60`. Streams a full logical SQL backup (init migration schema + data) straight to the browser as a download - no object storage/B2 needed. Tables/columns/FKs discovered at request time via `information_schema` (module tables included automatically, nothing hardcoded), topologically sorted for FK-safe restore order; **`_prisma_migrations` and `ModuleMigration` are excluded from the dump** (`getTables`) - both are build-time bookkeeping about the physical schema of the DB they live in, not portable content, and carrying a module's ledger into a restore made the target claim tables it doesn't have (see restore + runner self-heal, 2026-07-15); self-referencing tables (`MenuItem.parentId` and module equivalents) additionally row-ordered by BFS since plain FKs aren't deferrable. Restore target is always a fresh empty DB. Depends on `next.config.ts`'s `outputFileTracingIncludes` entry to ship the migration file into the function's Vercel bundle (a runtime `fs.readFileSync`, not a static import, so the file tracer needs the explicit hint). Dump logic lives in `lib/backup/dump.ts` (`buildBackupSql(db, schemaSql, generatedAt)`, takes a client so the round-trip test can drive it); the route is a thin auth + file-read wrapper. **The whole read phase runs inside ONE interactive transaction at `RepeatableRead`, `SET TRANSACTION READ ONLY` (2026-07-23)** - `maxWait` 10s, `timeout` 58s, deliberately just inside the route's 60s ceiling - so table discovery, every table's rows and the sequence counters all see a single snapshot. Without it a dump taken while the site was serving traffic could be internally inconsistent: a sequence read at N while a row using N+1 was read afterwards (restore rewinds the sequence and the next insert collides on a UNIQUE column), or a child row written mid-dump referencing a parent whose table had already been read (restore fails the FK). Neither shows up until RESTORE, which is the worst possible moment to find out. Consequently `BackupDb` now requires `$transaction` and a narrower `BackupTx` (just `$queryRawUnsafe`/`$executeRawUnsafe`) types the read helpers, because Prisma's interactive-transaction client deliberately has no `$transaction` of its own. Generated/identity columns are excluded (they can't be inserted into). **Sequences are dumped too** - a trailing `SELECT setval(...)` section - because they are not tables and nothing else would see them; without it a restored shop reset `shp_order_number_seq` to 1 and the next checkout generated an already-used `order_number` (UNIQUE) and hard-failed.

Value serialisation lives in `lib/backup/serialize.ts` (`serializeValue(value, ColumnType)`, unit-tested in `serialize.test.ts`). **Two invariants:** (1) the column's `information_schema` `udt_name` is the discriminator, NEVER the JS value shape - a `json`/`jsonb` column always emits a quoted JSON literal, a SQL-array column (udt starts with `_`) emits `ARRAY[...]::<elem>[]` with the cast (mixed-case enum element types quoted); (2) **it never guesses** - an unrecognised udt, or a value whose shape contradicts its column type, throws `UnsupportedColumnError` and aborts the whole dump (surfaced by the route as a 500 with a human message). The old silent "least-worst rendering" fall-through is what turned a small bug into an unrestorable backup: a bad literal is written happily and only fails at RESTORE time, months later, in an emergency. Bugs this caught: deciding on `Array.isArray` alone rendered `jsonb` array columns (`InfoPage.history`/`Layout.history`) as `text[]`, so restore died with `column "history" is of type jsonb but expression is of type text[]` (42804) on any site with a republished page; and `bytea` columns (`Passkey.publicKey`) came back from Prisma raw as a `Uint8Array`, not a `Buffer`, so the `Buffer.isBuffer` check missed them and they were JSON-stringified into garbage - every passkey silently unrestorable. Byte columns now accept any `Uint8Array`. **`date`/`time`/`timetz` gained branches of their own (2026-07-23, `TIME_OF_DAY`)**: `isSupportedUdtName` claimed them as supported while they sat in the string-only `TEXTUAL` set, and Prisma hands those columns back as a JS `Date`, so the first install carrying a DATE column would have thrown `UnsupportedColumnError` and aborted its own backup. They cannot share the `TEMPORAL` branch either - that emits a full ISO datetime, which a `date` column rejects for the time part and a `time` column rejects for the date part. Caught by the schema-coverage backstop's own rule that a claimed-supported udt must have a real branch.
- `POST /api/admin/backup/import` (protected-role) and `POST /api/setup/import-backup` (unauthenticated, but 404s the moment `setupCompleted && userCount > 0`, so it can never wipe a live site) - restore a `.sql` backup. Both delegate to `restoreDatabaseFromSql(sql, db = prisma)` in `lib/backup/restore.ts`, 100 MB cap. Destructive and total: TRUNCATE every table (bar the preserved ledgers `_prisma_migrations` **and `ModuleMigration`**) → replay the backup's INSERTs in file order → apply its `setval`s, all in ONE transaction, so a failure changes nothing. **`ModuleMigration` is preserved (2026-07-15)**, not wiped or restored - it records which module migrations THIS database physically ran; overwriting it with the source's ledger left a fresh restore target claiming module tables (created by migrations, absent from a backup's schema section) were applied, so the runner skipped them forever. INSERTs targeting a preserved table (an older backup made before the dump exclusion) are ignored. INSERTs for tables the target lacks (module not installed here) are skipped and reported; setvals for absent sequences likewise. **Version skew is checked BEFORE the TRUNCATE** (`assertSchemasMatch`): a column in the backup that the target lacks = backup is from a newer Cactus → refuse with a plain-English error telling the owner to update first (never silently drop the data); a target column that is NOT NULL with no default and absent from the backup = backup is from an older Cactus → refuse. Parsers (`splitSqlStatements`, `insertTargetTable`, `insertColumns`, `setvalTargetSequence`) unit-tested in `restore.parse.test.ts`. **Last step inside the transaction: `clearUnreadableSecrets(tx)` (`lib/backup/secrets.ts`)** - see below. `RestoreResult` therefore also carries `clearedSecrets: string[]` (plain English, shown by both restore UIs, which suppress their auto-redirect when it is non-empty) and `secretsChecked: boolean`. **After the transaction commits: `checkRestoredMediaStorage(db)` (`lib/backup/media-check.ts`, 2026-07-15)** adds `mediaWarnings: string[]`. A backup carries the Media catalogue but never the file bytes (those live in an external bucket - see dump), so a restore onto a site not connected to the source's storage leaves every image pointing at objects it can't serve. The check is **deterministic and network-free on purpose**: it never fetches the restored `url`s (they come from an uploaded file - fetching them would be an SSRF vector, especially on the pre-auth setup route), it just asks `isMediaProviderConfigured(provider)` (`lib/config/env.ts`) for each provider the restored `Media` rows use and warns about any this install has no credentials for. Conservative - it can't catch "right provider, wrong bucket" (creds look fine); that closes with the planned media-inclusive backup. Both restore UIs (`app/setup/page.tsx`, `app/cactus-admin/config/ConfigPageClient.tsx`) render `mediaWarnings` alongside `clearedSecrets` and hold the auto-redirect when either is non-empty. Unit-tested in `media-check.test.ts` (mock db + env, no network). The Backup download panel copy now also states the backup is database-only and the storage bucket must stay in place.
- **Encrypted-secret reconciliation on restore** - `lib/backup/secrets.ts`. `ENCRYPTION_KEY` is minted per install (`/api/setup/vercel-connect` generates a fresh random one), but a backup file is portable, so restoring onto a fresh install ALWAYS lands AES-256-GCM ciphertext (`lib/crypto/secrets.ts`) that this site's key cannot read - and a backup deliberately does not carry the old key. Left in place it is worse than absent: the `GithubAppConnection` row made the site report GitHub as connected while every call died with OpenSSL's `Unsupported state or unable to authenticate data`, and a two-factor enrolment pointed at a secret nobody could produce a code for. So after the INSERTs and setvals, still inside the transaction, every `*Encrypted` text column in every table (discovered from `information_schema`, so module columns following the convention are covered for free) is trial-decrypted. Values that are not `looksLikeEncryptedSecret()` are left alone - not ours, no guessing. Values that are ours but unreadable are neutralised: **NOT NULL column → the row is deleted** (a `GithubAppConnection` is nothing but its credentials), **nullable → set NULL**, plus `COMPANION_CLEARS` for state that depended on it (`User.totpSecretEncrypted` also clears `totpVerifiedAt`/`totpLastStep`, or the login offers an authenticator step that can never succeed). **`MemberTwoFactor` is the exception: rows are demoted to the `EMAIL` method, never deleted** - member sign-in 403s an account with no two-factor config at all (`Two-factor authentication is required but not yet configured`), so deleting would lock the member out exactly as thoroughly as the dead secret did; demotion keeps a real second factor (an emailed code) until they re-enrol. If `ENCRYPTION_KEY` is missing or malformed the sweep is skipped entirely (`secretsChecked: false`) - with no key there is no telling "wrong key" from "key not set yet", and wiping a site's secrets on the strength of a missing env var is not a trade worth making. Covered by the round-trip test's second case (restores under a different key and asserts the GitHub row is gone, the admin's TOTP flags are cleared, the member keeps an EMAIL factor, and content is untouched) and by `lib/crypto/secrets.test.ts` (no network, plain `npm test`).
- **Backup round-trip test** - `lib/backup/roundtrip.test.ts` + `lib/backup/vps-database.ts`. The only test that proves a backup actually restores, and the only one that catches bugs nobody predicted (it found the `bytea`/`Uint8Array` corruption on its first real run). Provisions its OWN throwaway databases on the self-hosted OVH Postgres VPS (moved off Neon 2026-07-22, no API key any more): SSHes in with `sshpass` using `OVH_SERVER`/`OVH_USER`/`OVH_PASSWORD` from root `.env`, creates role `cactus_rt_role_<stamp>` and database `cactus_rt_src_<stamp>`, applies the core init migration, seeds the awkward shapes on purpose (jsonb-holding-an-array on `InfoPage.history`/`Layout.history`, a populated `text[]` and an empty one, `bytea`, quotes-in-JSON), dumps it, restores the dump into `cactus_rt_dst_<stamp>` (a `CREATE DATABASE ... TEMPLATE` clone of the seeded source, replacing the old Neon copy-on-write branch), then compares an order-independent md5 content hash of EVERY table. Two further cases: restoring the same backup under a DIFFERENT `ENCRYPTION_KEY` (the normal case for a restore) clears every secret it cannot read and leaves the content alone; and a newer-Cactus backup is refused and changes nothing. Cleanup is unconditional: `afterAll` drops both databases and the role, and `dropStaleTestObjects` sweeps anything `cactus_rt_*` before AND after every run. `vps-database.ts` refuses to drop any name outside `/^cactus_rt_[a-z0-9_]{1,48}$/`, so the live `neondb` sharing that server is never named, opened or altered. Skipped unless `RUN_BACKUP_ROUNDTRIP=1` (set by `npm run test:backup-roundtrip`), so plain `npm test` never hits the network. **A skipped run is NOT a pass** - see `lib/backup/schema-coverage.test.ts` for the gap-filler that runs unconditionally.
- **Backup schema-coverage test** - `lib/backup/schema-coverage.test.ts`, runs in plain `npm test`, no key, no network, no skip. Statically parses every column type out of the init migration AND every `modules/*/migrations/*.sql` (both `CREATE TABLE` column lists and `ALTER TABLE ... ADD COLUMN` lines), maps the SQL type syntax to the `information_schema.udt_name` `lib/backup/serialize.ts` switches on, and asserts `isSupportedUdtName` (new export, pure lookup against `serialize.ts`'s own type sets, no behaviour change) is true for every one. Exists because the round-trip test's database-server requirement gives it an escape hatch (missing `OVH_*` details -> "skipped", not "failed", and a skipped suite still reports green) - this test has none: add a column of a type the serialiser has never seen (verified by deliberately injecting an `INET`/`TSVECTOR` column and confirming the run goes red) and `npm test` fails on the PR that added it, full stop.
- `GET/POST /api/admin/updates` - `config.manage`, `maxDuration 60`. GET: core update status by channel (public/beta), raises/clears the `core-update` notification, lists modules with updates when a core update exists. POST: acquires DeployLock, optionally queues module updates into the same deploy, `syncCoreFromUpstream`, arms the redeploy gate via `startDeferredRedeploy({committedSince})`; falls back to a deferred notification without Vercel credentials.
- `GET /api/admin/release-notes` - any authenticated session (no permission gate; upstream releases are public), `maxDuration 30`. `?page=N` (default 1) returns one page of the full upstream release history newest-first via `getReleaseNotesPage` (`lib/updates/core.ts`): `{ items: {version,tag,publishedAt,html,url}[], hasMore }`. Unlike `/api/admin/updates`, returns EVERY published release regardless of prerelease flag (About dialog is history, not an update prompt). Powers the infinite scroll in the About dialog's Release notes panel.
- `GET/POST /api/admin/layouts`; `GET/PATCH/DELETE /api/admin/layouts/[id]` - list/create/update/delete Layouts. **All five handlers require `layouts.manage`** - the two GETs used to accept any valid session, so an ordinary member's cookie could read every layout on the site. `GET` selects explicitly (no `publishedData`, no `history` - the latter is up to ten whole Puck payloads per layout, previously shipped to the browser on every list load), orders published-first then `updatedAt` desc, and calls `ensureLayoutsCurrent()` so an admin-only site still gets the post-update prune. `POST` rejects an unknown `type` (`isKnownLayoutType`) and seeds `defaultConditionsForLayout(type)` when the caller sends none. `PATCH` validates every field it accepts (non-empty `name`, `status` in the enum, known `type`, integer `priority`, shaped `displayConditions`) instead of handing them to Prisma raw and returning a 500; with `status: 'published'` it refuses unless the layout is left with ≥1 **complete** include condition (`isCompleteRule` - a rule with a blank value shows nothing), then archives the previous `publishedData` into `history` (cap 10, mirrors the pages publish route) before writing the new `publishedData`/`publishedAt`/`publishedById`.
- `POST /api/admin/layouts/[id]/duplicate` (`layouts.manage`) - forks any layout: `"<name> (Copy)"`, counting up to `(Copy 2)`, `(Copy 3)` … when that name is taken, same type/description/builderData/priority, always `draft` with empty display conditions. Surfaced as a Duplicate button on every card in the admin Layouts list (alongside Edit/Preview/Delete, no longer starter-only).
- `GET /api/admin/layouts/[id]/history` (`layouts.manage`) - `?index=live|N` for full blobs, no param for the version list. Mirrors `GET /api/admin/pages/[id]/history`. Restoring a **published** layout re-publishes through `PATCH` (`status: 'published'`), so the version it replaces is archived and the tab's "Live" entry stays true; a bare `builderData` PATCH would have put the restored content live while `publishedData` still described the old one.
- `POST /api/admin/layouts/[id]/publish` - **removed** (v0.5.401). Zero callers, and it flipped `status: 'published'` while skipping the display-conditions guard and never writing `publishedData`/`history`: a back door that could put a layout live with no rules and no history. Publishing goes through `PATCH`.
- `POST /api/admin/layouts/[id]/use-sitewide` - **removed**. It only ever accepted `isStarter` rows, which no longer exist. A layout is published site-wide from the builder's Conditions tab like any other.
- `GET/POST /api/admin/saved-blocks` (`pages.read`/`pages.write`); `DELETE /api/admin/saved-blocks/[id]` (`pages.write`) - reusable Puck block snapshots (`SavedBlock` model), shared by the page and layout editors' Saved Blocks tab.
- `GET/POST/DELETE /api/admin/media` - **GET single item: `?id=<mediaId>` (2026-07-23)** short-circuits ahead of the listing and returns just that row (`id`, `key`, `url`, `altText`, `originalName`, `mimeType`, url passed through `signAssetUrl`), still shaped as the usual `{ items: [...], total, page, perPage, hasMore }` envelope so callers need no second code path; an unknown id returns an empty `items` array rather than a 404. The parameter was previously ignored, so anything asking for one item by id (the OG-image and media-picker previews) silently got the default newest-first listing and rendered the last-uploaded image instead. GET list (session only) via the shared `queryMediaLibrary`/`parseLibraryQuery` (`lib/media/library-query.ts`): params `folder` (id / omitted=root / `all`), `q` search, `tag`, `type=all|image|other`, `sort=newest|oldest|name|name_desc|largest|smallest`, `filter=all|in-use|unused`, **`optimisable=1`** (raster, not SVG, `optimised=false` - the same predicate `computeLibraryStats` counts for the Optimisable tile, in SQL; the tile's drill-down used to set `type=image` and so listed every already-optimised image beside the handful still to do), `page`/`perPage`; returns `{ items, total, page, perPage, hasMore }`, each item carrying `inUse` (`loadMediaUsageIndex`/`isMediaInUse`), `folderId` and `tags[]`, and each item's `url` passed through `signAssetUrl` (a no-op for everything but 3D models, which the Worker refuses untokened - the library's own picker previews one in a viewer); the default `all` usage tab paginates at the DB (count + skip/take), the in-use/unused tabs load-classify-slice. Backs `MediaLibrary.tsx`. POST upload (`media.upload`; active provider selected AND configured; content-sniff via sharp) now also reads a `folderId` form field and threads its `resolveFolderPath` into `uploadMedia`/`saveMediaRecord`. This serverless multipart path is now the FALLBACK only (SVGs, non-S3 providers, or when the direct path is unavailable/fails); it's size-guarded at `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES` (4 MB) from `lib/media/limits.ts`. **The key now keeps the uploaded filename** (`buildLibraryUploadKey` in `lib/media/upload.ts`, passed to `uploadMedia`'s new `presetKey` argument): the exact-name key is used when no `Media` row already holds it, else `-2`, `-3` … up to 50, and only then the old `<nanoid>-<label>` form. `Media.originalName` is unchanged (still the verbatim name for display); this is about what the bucket and the served URL say.
- **Direct-to-Worker upload (50 MB cap - `MAX_DIRECT_UPLOAD_BYTES`, raster images on S3-compatible providers; 3D models ride the same road, see below):** client-side `uploadOneFile` (`lib/media/upload-client.ts`, driven by `MediaLibrary.enqueueFiles` via the shared upload queue, 6 files in flight at once after all name-clash prompts are answered; takes an optional `onProgress` fraction callback) routes raster types (`RASTER_DIRECT_TYPES`: jpeg/png/webp/gif) through: (1) `POST /api/admin/media/upload-url` - `media.upload`; returns `{ available, uploadUrl, key, token }` when the active provider is S3-compatible (`isS3Provider`) AND `CLOUDFLARE_WORKER_URL` is set, else `{ available:false }`; `key` from `buildLibraryUploadKey` (exact filename, deduped `-2`/`-3` … against existing `Media.key`s, nanoid form only as a last resort), `token` from `signUploadToken`. An optional **`replaceId`** aims the same machinery at an item that already exists (see `[id]/replace`): the key comes from `planMediaReplacement` instead of `buildKey`, and `{ available:false }` also when the row sits on a provider the site has since moved off (the Worker only carries the ACTIVE provider's credentials, so those fall to the serverless path, which writes with the app's own) (`lib/media/upload-token.ts`, HMAC over `key\n<exp>` with a key derived from `SESSION_SECRET` via `deriveUploadSigningKey`, 15-min TTL). (2) Browser `PUT`s the file bytes to `<worker>/<key>` with `Authorization: Bearer <token>`; the media Worker (`workers/media-worker/index.ts`) verifies the token, resolves the provider from the key path, and does a SigV4 PUT (real payload hash, body buffered) to storage. **The Worker takes the stored content-type from the KEY's extension, never from the client's `Content-Type` header** (the key is covered by the signature and its extension comes from an already-validated MIME type, so it's the one type claim a client can't forge - trusting the header let a `media.upload` holder store `text/html` + script and have it served back as executable HTML from the media origin). It requires a `Content-Length`, rejects anything over 50 MB before buffering, rejects a body whose real length disagrees with it, and refuses SVG outright (only the serverless path sanitises SVG). On GET it always sends `X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff`, echoes an upstream content-type only if it's a known image type, and serves anything else as `application/octet-stream` + `Content-Disposition: attachment` - which retroactively defuses any object poisoned before this. (3) `POST /api/admin/media/record` - `media.upload`; **requires the signed upload `token` back** (same signature the Worker checked, so a row can only point at a key this session was issued) and derives `mimeType` from the signed key rather than the body; size clamped to 50 MB; writes the `Media` row via `saveMediaRecord`. **`sizeBytes` is no longer taken from the body either** (2026-07-19): the body figure is the client's own `file.size`, which describes the file it meant to send rather than the object that landed, and on this path the bytes never pass through the app to be measured - `confirmedSizeBytes` (`lib/media/upload.ts`) HEADs the object and records the real length, keeping the claimed value only when the provider cannot say. The body value still serves the 50 MB cap check. `[id]/replace`'s direct path does the same via `adoptReplacementBlob`. Core's `/record` stays **image-only** (`isRasterDirectType`) even though `contentTypeForKey` now types model extensions too: the library's own routes upload photographs, and the module that uploads models signs its own keys and records its own rows. Any failure in this chain falls back to the serverless path, so an un-redeployed Worker degrades to current behaviour - **but the Worker must be redeployed (Settings → Media → Deploy Worker) for the upload/serve hardening to take effect.** The Worker gains `OPTIONS`/`PUT` handlers + CORS + `UPLOAD_SIGNING_SECRET` env, pushed on Worker redeploy by `deploy-worker/route.ts`. `uploadErrorMessage` (`limits.ts`) still special-cases the serverless 413. DELETE `?id=&force=` (`media.delete`; 409 + reference list unless `force`). Reference check is `getMediaReferences` in `lib/media/upload.ts` (logo/favicon light+dark, page OG images, member avatars, data exports, and Puck builder JSON) - kept in step with `lib/media/references.ts`. Its haystack hit is now labelled **"page, layout or module content"**, since the same haystack carries module-contributed references and a substring hit can't say which matched.
- `PATCH /api/admin/media/[id]` - `media.upload`. Rename and/or move one item. Body `{ newName?, targetFolderId?, collision? }` → `moveOrRenameMedia`; a name clash under the default `error` mode returns `409 { collision, name }`. **Also handles a metadata-only edit** `{ altText?: string|null, isDecorative?: boolean }` (present WITHOUT `newName`/`targetFolderId`): a plain `prisma.media.update` (no collision path) - trims/nulls empty alt text, and forces `altText=null` when `isDecorative` is true. Backs the detail panel's alt-text editor + Decorative toggle (`MediaDetailPanel.onSaveMeta` → `MediaLibrary.saveMeta`). `DELETE /api/admin/media/[id]` unchanged (path-param twin of the query DELETE).
- `POST /api/admin/media/move` - `media.upload`. Bulk move. Body `{ ids, targetFolderId, collision? }`; `error` mode stops at the first clash with `409 { collision, name, id, moved, skipped }`, other modes (suffix/replace/skip) resolve inline. Backs drag-drop + Move to….
- `POST /api/admin/media/duplicate` - `media.upload`. Body `{ ids, targetFolderId }`; clones each blob into the target as a new row (paste-copy), names auto-suffixed on clash, no reference rewrite (nothing points at a fresh copy).
- `POST /api/admin/media/name-check` - `media.upload`. Body `{ folderId, names[] }` → `{ clashes: [{ name, existingId, suggestedName }] }`. Asked by the library's uploader BEFORE any bytes move, so an upload whose name is already taken in the destination can offer Replace / Keep both / Skip / Cancel instead of silently auto-suffixing. `suggestedName` is the free `name-1.ext` form (`checkUploadName` in `lib/media/organise.ts`) - hyphen, not " (1)", because it ends up in the storage key and so in the public url.
- `GET/POST /api/admin/media/folders` - GET (session) returns every folder (flat, with direct-child `mediaCount`) + `rootCount`; POST (`media.upload`) creates a folder `{ name, parentId? }`. `GET/PATCH/DELETE /api/admin/media/folders/[id]` - GET (session) the cascade-delete summary `{ folders, media, inUseNames }`; PATCH (`media.upload`) rename `{ name }` OR move `{ parentId }` (string/null) via `moveFolder` - rejects cycles + destination name clashes, relocates every descendant item either way; DELETE (`media.delete`) permanent cascade of the whole subtree (blobs + rows, via idempotent `deleteMany` so a re-submitted confirm no longer throws P2025).
- `GET/POST /api/admin/media/tags` - GET (session) all tags with counts; POST (`media.upload`) upsert-create `{ name }`. `PUT /api/admin/media/[id]/tags` - `media.upload`. Body `{ tags: string[] }` replaces the item's tag set (missing tags created on the fly, removed ones unlinked, Tag rows kept for reuse).
- `DELETE /api/admin/media/[id]` - path-param twin of the above DELETE (`DELETE /api/admin/media/<id>`); same session/permission/reference-check/deletion logic. (The admin media UI now deletes via `bulk-delete` for both single and multi; this route remains for any direct/path-param callers.)
- `POST /api/admin/media/bulk-delete` - `media.delete`. Body `{ ids: string[], force?: boolean }`; per-id same reference check as the single-delete routes (skips items still in use unless `force`), continues through the rest of the list regardless of any one item's outcome. Returns `{ deleted: string[], skipped: {id, references}[], notFound: string[] }`. Backs the media library's delete flow - single (detail panel / context menu) and multi-select bar (`MediaLibrary.tsx`).
- `POST /api/admin/media/optimise` - `media.upload`. Body `{ mediaId }`. Downloads the item's original bytes, runs sharp (`resize` fit-inside max 1024px, no enlargement → lossless `webp` effort 6, `animated:true`), stores the result as a new media row and returns `{ optimised:true, id, url, before, after }`; if the WebP came out no smaller it keeps the original and returns `{ optimised:false, before, after }`. Original row left untouched. Used by the Branding tab's logo "Optimise" button.
- `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/optimise` - `media.upload`. Optimises a single media item **in place** via `optimiseMediaInPlace` (`lib/media/upload.ts`): re-encodes to lossy WebP (`quality:82, effort:6, animated:true`, no downscale), and if smaller keeps the same `Media.id` while pointing `key`/`url`/`mimeType`/`sizeBytes` at the new blob, sets `Media.optimised`, rewrites any url/key refs embedded in Puck `InfoPage`/`Layout` builder JSON **and runs every module-registered `core.media-reference-rewriters` provider** (so `shp_product_media`/`svr_option_values` urls follow the blob), then deletes the pre-optimise blob. Returns the `OptimiseResult` (`{optimised:true, before, after}` or `{optimised:false, reason, before?, after?}`). Skips SVG/non-raster and already-optimised rows. Distinct from `/optimise` above (which mints a new row for Branding). Backs the media library's per-card "Optimise" button.
- `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/edit` - `media.upload`. Crop/edit one raster image via `editMediaImage` (`lib/media/upload.ts`). Body `{ crop: {left, top, width, height}, mode: 'replace'|'new', newName? }`; crop rect is in the source image's own pixels (clamped to bounds server-side). Downloads the original, `sharp().extract(rect)`, re-encodes in the source's own format (`encodeCrop`: jpeg/png/webp/gif/avif, else WebP; reads first frame only so an animated source becomes a still). `replace` swaps the blob under the existing row (same `Media.id`, `optimised` reset to false, rewrites embedded url/key refs in Puck JSON, deletes the pre-edit blob - the optimise-in-place pattern). `new` uploads the crop and `saveMediaRecord`s a fresh row in the same folder, original untouched. Returns `{ ok, item }`. Skips SVG/non-raster. Backs the media library's Edit image tool (`MediaImageEditor.tsx`).
- `POST /api/admin/media/bulk-optimise` - `media.upload`. Body `{ ids: string[] }`. Runs `optimiseMediaInPlace` over each id sequentially (each re-encode is CPU-heavy), one failure never aborts the rest. Returns `{ optimised: string[], skipped: {id, reason}[], failed: {id, error}[], bytesSaved }`. Backs the media library's multi-select "Optimise" bar (`MediaLibrary.tsx`), which since 2026-07-20 calls it once per id through `runBulkImageJob`'s 6-worker pool rather than handing it the whole selection - the route is unchanged and still accepts any length.
- `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/aspect` - `media.upload`. Change one raster image's aspect ratio via `changeMediaAspectRatio` (`lib/media/upload.ts`). Body `{ ratioW, ratioH, fill: {kind:'blur'|'colour'|'transparent', colour?}, mode:'replace'|'new', newName? }` (parsed by the shared `parseAspectRequest`, `lib/media/aspect-request.ts`; ratio capped at 20:1). **Pads, never crops or stretches**: geometry from the pure `planAspectChange` (`lib/media/aspect-plan.ts`) grows only the short axis so every source pixel survives, then `blur` composites the whole image over a cover-cropped+blurred copy of itself, while `colour`/`transparent` use `sharp().extend()`. Returns `{ ok, changed:true, item, width, height, downscaled }`, or `{ ok, changed:false, reason }` when the image is already that ratio or a JPEG asked for transparency (`supportsTransparentFill`). Skips SVG/non-raster. Backs `MediaAspectDialog.tsx`.
- `POST /api/admin/media/bulk-aspect` - `media.upload`. Body `{ ids: string[] }` + the same aspect fields as `[id]/aspect`. Runs `changeMediaAspectRatio` over each id sequentially, one failure never aborts the rest. Returns `{ changed: string[], skipped: {id, reason}[], failed: {id, error}[] }`. Backs the media library's multi-select "Change ratio…" bar, called once per id through `runBulkImageJob`'s 6-worker pool since 2026-07-20 (route unchanged, still accepts any length).
- `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/resize` - `media.upload`. Scale one raster image down via `resizeMediaImage` (`lib/media/upload.ts`). Body `{ width?, height?, mode:'replace'|'new', newName? }` (parsed by the shared `parseResizeRequest`, `lib/media/resize-request.ts`; at least one side required, each capped at `MAX_RESIZE_DIMENSION` 20000px). **Uniform downscale, never an upscale**: geometry from the pure `planResize` (`lib/media/resize-plan.ts`) fits the image inside the box keeping its own ratio, so the box is a ceiling not a target - `sharp().resize(w, h, {fit:'inside', withoutEnlargement:true})`, then `encodeToMime` keeps the source format. Output dimensions are **re-measured off the encoded bytes**, not taken from the plan (`fit:'inside'` can land a pixel under the box). Persists via the shared `persistDerivedImage` (same replace/new semantics as `[id]/edit` and `[id]/aspect`). Returns `{ ok, changed:true, item, width, height, capped, before, after }`, or `{ ok, changed:false, reason }` when the image already fits inside the box. Skips SVG/non-raster. Backs `MediaResizeDialog.tsx`.
- `POST /api/admin/media/[id]/replace` - `media.upload`. **Swap one item's file for a freshly uploaded one, keeping the item**: same `Media.id`, name, folder, alt text, decorative flag and tags, so every page/product/setting pointing at it keeps working and simply shows the new picture (the difference between this and "upload the new one, delete the old one", which breaks every page the old one was on). Two request shapes mirroring the two upload paths: **multipart `{ file }`** (serverless fallback, `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES` 4 MB; the bytes pass through here so `validateUpload` sees them - real image, SVG sanitised) → `replaceMediaFile`; or **json `{ key, token, sizeBytes }`** (direct path, 50 MB) → `adoptReplacementBlob`, where the client already PUT the bytes to the Worker at a key this app signed. The direct path takes nothing that decides where the row points from the body (the /record rule): type comes from the signed key via `contentTypeForKey`, the token is re-verified, and the key is re-checked against `planMediaReplacement` - same directory (a token from a *plain* upload would otherwise quietly move the item to another folder), and for an exact-named item the one key it may occupy at all. Storage is the provider the ROW lives on, not the active selection (503 if that one's creds are absent). `optimised` resets to false (a freshly picked file has not been through the optimiser, exactly as a fresh upload of it would be). Returns `{ ok, item }`. Backs the media library's Replace button (card hover 🔄 / detail-panel footer / context menu).
- `planMediaReplacement` (`lib/media/upload.ts`) decides where a replacement blob lands: the item's own provider/folder/name, with only the extension following the new bytes' type (`withExtensionForMime`, so a JPEG replacing "hero.png" is filed and displayed as "hero.jpg"). **An exact-named item (`isExactNameKey`, see `lib/media/keys.ts`) may only be replaced by a file of its own type** → `MediaReplaceTypeError` → 409 with a plain reason, refused at `/upload-url` too so the client isn't told only after pushing the whole file up. Reason: its name IS its key, so a new extension means a new key. Module-owned url columns are now rewritten too (the `core.media-reference-rewriters` extension point), but the refusal is **kept as defence-in-depth** - an exact-named item may be referenced by a module that has registered no rewriter, and a type-changing replace would leave that reference pointing at the blob the swap then deletes, so the image would vanish from that surface while sitting intact in the library.
- `rewriteMediaReferencesInContent` (`lib/media/upload.ts`) swaps a media item's old url/key for its new one inside Puck builder JSON (`InfoPage` + `Layout`, both `builderData` and `publishedData`), then runs every module rewriter.
